Current Affairs Commentary

The Seriousness of the Chahar North Issue 12

Since the Japanese and puppet troops occupied six counties of Chahar, the essence of Chahar Province, half of the area has been lost, and the Suiyuan border is becoming increasingly critical. Recently, it was reported that the authorities in Peiping are discussing with the Japanese side to resolve the Chahar North issue and have reached a compromise on the local administration of the six counties, that is, the candidates for the county magistrates of the six counties will be dispatched by the Mongolian Political Affairs Committee and then formally appointed by the Chahar Provincial Government. Whether this matter can be resolved in this way is still a question. Judging from the Japanese advance, they must take one step at a time in the Inner Mongolia area, and it is feared that there is no other peaceful way to stop them from advancing along the PingSui Railway. Japan obviously has a plan to conquer all of our Inner Mongolian territory and develop towards Outer Mongolia and attack the Soviet Union. The military actions in Chahar North are the beginning of this.

In terms of the geographical situation of the six counties in Chahar North, the area controls the Zhangku Highway, which is the throat of China's transportation with Outer Mongolia and Soviet Russia. The Zhangku Highway is cut off, and Sino-Russian commerce cannot proceed. There is no way to communicate between Kulun and Peiping. Zhangbei can control the PingSui Railway when it goes south, and the PingSui Railway is the lifeline of Inner Mongolia and the provinces of Chahar and Suiyuan. Japan's plan is not only to connect the South Manchuria Railway with the Beining Railway, but also to connect the Beining and PingSui Railways, so that Japanese troops coming from Dalian can reach Inner Mongolia directly via the South Manchuria, Beining, and PingSui Railways, and can also connect to the Zhangku Highway from various roads, stationing troops on the border of Outer Mongolia and threatening Kulun. If this plan is realized, Korea and Suiyuan can have direct traffic, and Inner and Outer Mongolia and the provinces of Sui, Jin, Shaanxi, Hebei will have no peaceful days.

Japan's plan to conquer Inner and Outer Mongolia originally had a concrete plan. The occupation of the six counties of Guyuan was the beginning of the implementation of this plan. In the eyes of the Doihara generation, the creation of the so-called "Mongolian Country" is more important than the "Manchukuo" because only by controlling Mongolia can the goal of controlling the Asian continent be achieved. What Asian history has shown is that only the forces north of the Great Wall can control China for a long time. Therefore, when the puppet state of Manchuria was created, the Japanese divided the Mongolian people in Manchuria into an "Xing'an Autonomous Province" and gave them considerable autonomy to make it a base point for the "Mongolian Country" plan. There are two or three million Mongolians in Xing'an Province, which is half of the total Mongolian population. The Japanese used Hulun (Hailar) as the base for inciting the Mongolian people to break away from China. On the one hand, they threatened Outer Mongolia, and on the other hand, they lured Inner Mongolia. Fortunately, the princes of Inner Mongolia were still able to distinguish between friends and enemies and did not fall into the Japanese conspiracy in the past. Outer Mongolia relied on Soviet Russia for support. Although it has repeatedly made concessions to the Japanese and Manchurian invasion, it is quite limited. Now that Japan has reached out to Chahar Province, not only is the regime in the Bai Ling Temple area in grave danger, but Kulun is also like a sharp sword in the abdomen, and its life is in danger. The situation is more serious than the September 18th Incident.

Japan's means of dealing with our country are the most cruel, namely, creating many puppet states in our country's territory, directly ruled by Japanese officials and occupied by Japanese troops. The puppet state of Manchuria is a completed puppet. The so-called "Hebei East Anti-Communist Government" is the core of the second puppet. Japan not only has no intention of abolishing this pseudo-organization, but also wants to incorporate the Ji-Cha Political Affairs Committee to complete its so-called "North China State" plan. In Inner Mongolia, Japan is also using the Xing'an Autonomous Province as the core to create another expanded puppet organization. The Mongolian Political Affairs Committee has already become the target of the Japanese to seize as their own. Once the six counties of Guyuan are lost, it will be difficult to return them. In the future, if the area south of the desert unfortunately becomes the second Manchuria, the northern crisis will be so severe. Can the people of the country still sit idly by and not think about rising up to save the situation?

Records of the Legislative Yuan Meeting: Approval of the 23rd Year Supplementary Budget; No Need to Formulate a Real Estate Mortgage Law 13

Nanjing: The Legislative Yuan held its 43rd regular meeting on the morning of the 17th. Seventy-one members, including Zhou Wei, attended. Sun Ke presided, with Liang Hancao as Secretary-General. The following matters were resolved: The supplementary budget for the 23rd year for national ordinary revenue and expenditure was approved as is. The agreement and detailed rules for the exchange of parcels between post offices in Malaya and China were approved as is. The Executive Yuan's request to formulate a Real Estate Property Rights Registration Law was resolved that the Land Law and its implementation regulations already have provisions for real estate property rights registration, and there is no need to formulate a separate single law. The Executive Yuan's request to formulate an Auction Law was resolved that regarding auction procedures, the Yuan is drafting a Compulsory Execution Law, which should include appropriate provisions. The Executive Yuan's request to formulate a Real Estate Mortgage Law was resolved that the Civil Code already has provisions for real estate mortgages, and there is no need to formulate a separate single law. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 17th)

Nanjing: The Executive Yuan consulted the Legislative Yuan, stating that regarding the exercise of mortgage rights, it is permissible in areas where land surveys are completed and the registration system is relatively complete, to handle matters in accordance with Article 873, Paragraph 1 of the Civil Code, without being bound by Interpretation No. 493 of the Judicial Yuan. Additionally, factory machinery can be regarded as accessories in accordance with Article 1, Paragraph 1 of the Civil Code and mortgaged together with real estate. The Executive Yuan requested the Judicial Yuan to investigate and interpret this matter. Now, the Ministry of Finance reports that new monetary policies are being implemented and methods should be added to increase the activity capacity of general banks, and also plans to establish a special organization to handle real estate mortgage business to facilitate financial circulation. Regarding real estate mortgage laws and regulations, it is hoped that the Judicial and Legislative Yuans will revise and formulate them as early as possible to provide a basis for regulating finance and rescuing the industrial and commercial crisis. Accordingly, the Legislative Yuan was consulted for review. The Legislative Yuan's meeting on the 17th resulted in a decision that, except for the fact that the Civil Code already has provisions for real estate mortgages and there is no need to formulate a separate single law, two additional points were interpreted: The original intention of Article 873, Paragraph 1 of the Civil Code is that if the mortgage creditor's debt has reached the repayment period and has not been repaid, they may petition the court to sell the mortgaged property through auction procedures to show caution, without needing to go through a final judgment. The Legislative Yuan is drafting a Compulsory Execution Law, and it also intends to add appropriate provisions regarding auction procedures. As for whether Interpretation No. 493 of the Judicial Yuan should be changed, since the Executive Yuan has consulted the Judicial Yuan to handle it, the Legislative Yuan is not in a position to comment. The meaning of accessories is already defined in Article 68 of the Civil Code. If the factory machinery mentioned complies with the provisions of that article, it can naturally be regarded as accessories. Since the Executive Yuan has consulted the Judicial Yuan for interpretation, the Legislative Yuan does not need to comment. It is noted that this case is because the Judicial Yuan, regarding the mortgagee's request to auction the mortgaged property, once used Interpretation No. 493, requiring that it could only be done after a final judgment. However, courts often delay in resolving such debt cases, causing those who invest in real estate to suffer losses, and the real estate mortgage business also declined as a result. The Executive Yuan's request for the Legislative Yuan to formulate a Real Estate Mortgage Law was to seek a remedy for this matter and to regulate social finance. However, the Legislative Yuan believes that Article 873 of the Civil Code stipulates that a mortgagee's auction of mortgaged property must be applied for to the court, and the original intention was to seek caution in the procedures. Interpretation No. 493 of the Judicial Yuan seems to be a misunderstanding. Real estate mortgages are already provided for in the Civil Code. The reason for the decline in real estate mortgage business is not due to the lack of a Real Estate Mortgage Law, but entirely due to the constraints of Interpretation No. 493 of the Judicial Yuan. Therefore, the meeting on the 17th decided that there is no need to formulate a Real Estate Mortgage Law. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 17th)

During the Legislative Yuan's meeting on the 17th to review the draft Auction Law, the Civil Law Committee believed that the auction procedure would be appropriately stipulated in the Compulsory Execution Law being drafted, so there was no need to formulate a separate single law. Some legislators then questioned the Civil Law Committee, stating that various parties urgently need an Auction Law, such as customs auctions of seized smuggled goods and bank pawnshops auctioning overdue mortgages. Will the auction procedures be fully covered in the future Compulsory Execution Law? Besides the application of judicial punishment, is the Compulsory Execution Law applicable to other dispositions? The Civil Law Committee was requested to explain. Otherwise, an Auction Law should still be formulated to meet the needs of all parties. The Civil Law Committee replied that the opinions expressed by the committee members could be used as references when drafting the Compulsory Execution Law. The review report was then passed, rejecting the formulation of an Auction Law. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 17th)

Bandit Liu Wanders; The County Seat of Xingtang is in Danger 18

Tianjin: According to the captured bandits of Liu Guitang's bandit gang moving south, there are more than 1,700 bandits. Along the way, they forced farmers to join, expanding to more than 3,000. They have more than 2,000 firearms of various sizes, countless horses, and six cannons. Xingtang, Tangxian, Weixian, Lingshou, and Quyang have all been ravaged by the bandits. On the 15th, more than 700 bandits sneaked into Xingtang. More than 180 members of the Yangjiazhuang militia fought back. Due to the disparity in numbers, half were surrounded and disarmed. The remnants retreated to Wangting Town, 25 miles north of the city, waiting for reinforcements. The bandits have occupied Koutou Town, 50 miles north of the city. The county seat of Xingtang is in danger. The 53rd Army of the 29th Army is still pursuing and suppressing them. Because the bandits split up and fled, the army's pursuit target is lost. More than 600 mounted bandits were found at the junction of Fuping and Lingshou. The 655th Regiment engaged them at Wangkuaizhen on the 15th, killing many. The bandits took advantage of the night to cross the South Sha River and fled south through Pingyanggou. The bandits in southern Hebei are all stirring at the news. (Special dispatch on the 17th)

Tianjin: Liu Guitang's bandit gang outside Xifengkou in Zunhua was defeated by the joint attack of the puppet army inside and outside the pass and the Japanese army and fled east to Maguyu Shuangtangou. The puppet army is still in pursuit. The bandits suffered heavy casualties in the battle of Zhuma Village. When they fled in collapse, they set fire to more than ten villages and looted all the property. More than 600 remnants were led by Zhang Haijiao. (Special dispatch on the 17th)

Internal Interpretation of Doubts Regarding the Regulations for Supervising Temples 29

Nanjing: The Ministry of Interior interpreted several doubts regarding the Regulations for Supervising Temples: 1. If the abbot is dismissed, expelled, or sent to court, the generation of his successor will be handled in accordance with Item 19 of Interpretation No. 817 of the Judicial Yuan. He cannot reside in the temple without the permission of the current abbot. If he forcibly returns to the temple, he can be sent to court for investigation. 2. If there is an abbot in a temple who does not abide by the rules of conduct, and the church to which he belongs decides to request the government to dismiss him. 3. An abbot who is dismissed for not abiding by the rules of conduct cannot return to the temple to cause trouble. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 17th)

On Expanding Borders 53

— Intolerable

The greatest crisis in the world today lies in the demands of a few ambitious countries to expand their borders. Therefore, the border issue has become the most concerning issue worldwide. The renowned American journalist Lewis Rex Miller recently wrote an essay examining this issue with an objective and broad perspective. Although at first glance it may seem to carry a hint of American imperialism, its central idea truly leans towards global harmony. The original article was published in the Christian Science Monitor, and the following is an abridged translation:

Rasmond Robins, an American socio-economic scholar, once gave a speech entitled "The Last Frontier." By "The Last Frontier," he was referring to Alaska and the Klondike. Indeed, in the long history of the expansion of the American continent, these two places can truly be said to be the last frontiers. Americans generally feel that the determination of these borders has created a historical turning point. From then on, brave pioneers no longer aspired to place any newly uncultivated land under American rule.

Almost simultaneously, just before the World War, the division of the African continent by European colonial powers, except for Abyssinia and Liberia, had been completed. All the islands in the Pacific Ocean were seized by the great powers, and acquiring new territories in the Asian continent was no longer as easy as before. Everyone felt that the expansion of political borders was encountering increasing obstacles, which would inevitably lead to conflicts between countries. Indeed, the World War was caused by this.

Today, nearly twenty years have passed since the possibility of completely exhausting the expansion of borders, but many countries are still expanding their borders at an alarming rate. These so-called borders are not only political but also economic and cultural.

The most obvious and most often thought of is the "political border." Japan has expanded its borders beyond Manchuria and is currently working to place a large part of North China under its de facto control. Italy has expanded its borders to the more southern parts of Libya and is currently striving to incorporate Abyssinia into its colonial territory. These two are prominent examples of expanding borders by traditional military means.

Less obvious is the expansion of the "strategic border." In the winter of 1934, Baldwin declared that Britain would take the Rhine River as its border. When he said this, he did not mean that Britain would seize the territory and administration of Belgium and the Netherlands, but rather that due to the development of aviation, such a huge change had taken place in the military aspect that Britain could no longer rely on the traditional first line of defense! The fleet in the English Channel and the North Sea! Instead, it had to find more distant bases and prepare to resist attacks far from its borders.

Even more elusive than political and strategic borders are "economic borders." In a sense, we can say that every time an Easterner buys a Ford car, the American border expands once. The world market is no different from a large battlefield, and the major business competitors are all in this battlefield, forever seeking to expand their scope of operations. The expansion of this economic border is so significant that it can almost be said that any country is included within the borders of any other country. Clear evidence can be seen from the American dining table. Cuba (sugar), China and Japan (rice, porcelain), Ireland (linen), Italy and Spain (olive oil), Dutch East Indies (pepper), Mexico (vanilla), Costa Rica (bananas), Ceylon (cinnamon), Arabia and Turkey (dates and figs), and the economic borders of many other countries, have they not already rushed into American dining rooms?

In this situation, the expansion of borders will continue until the borders virtually cease to exist. Although the increase in tariffs creates serious barriers to the exchange of goods, it cannot prevent the inevitable international communication. The expansion of economic borders is absolutely necessary for any modern country. The result should not be conflict, but mutual satisfaction.

If the expansion of economic borders reaches the point where the borders between countries are almost indistinguishable, then "cultural borders" are naturally even more difficult to discern. Tariff barriers and censorship are absolutely incapable of resisting languages and scripts. Speeches broadcast on shortwave radio in Boston can be heard by audiences in the Americas, Europe, Africa, and Asia. The difficulties of written language can be overcome by translation.

A culture more consistent than previously known is currently widely prevalent on the surface of the Earth. Europeans feel that Europe is becoming Americanized. Americans feel that America is becoming Europeanized. Asians and Africans are adopting Western civilization, at least in material terms. Japan, which has always regarded Westernization as terrible, has now become the most enthusiastic promoter of Western civilization in the Eastern world. The natives of Africa know how to use modern films to open up their backwardness, while European artists use the handicrafts of primitive peoples as norms for their works. English speakers currently account for more than eleven percent of the world's population.

In the field of natural science, astonishing border expansions have been created in recent years. The new telescope on Mount Palomar in California will undoubtedly reveal the universe of objects previously considered speculative. Undersea exploration has discovered previously unknown patterns of animal life. Aircraft have soared to previously unattainable altitudes. The polar regions have become hunting grounds for daring aviators and explorers.

"Moral borders" have also expanded greatly. Respect for individual freedom has led almost every country to abolish slavery. The last barrier of legal slavery existing under the sun has collapsed with the recent abolition movement of the Emperor of Abyssinia. The progress of humanitarianism and the awareness of the status of women has eliminated many陋習 (lòu xí, bad customs) such as widow immolation in India. Disgust for the long-standing military system has led to the establishment of institutions such as the Peace Court, the League of Nations, and the Kellogg-Briand Pact.

Borders are expanding without limit and will eventually cease to be borders. If our goal is to acquire a certain territory or a certain market, the result will certainly be conflict. But if our goal is in an unlimited territory concerning the common welfare of all mankind, then the result will not be conflict but cooperation. (Translated from Lewis Rex Miller's essay)

Page 8

Naval Four-Power Conference Passes Shipbuilding Notification Proposal Qualitative Restrictions to be Discussed After Japan's Withdrawal 54

The First Committee of the London Naval Conference met this afternoon, without the presence of Japanese representatives. It was agreed that shipbuilding procedures should be mutually notified in advance. This is the first compromise reached by the conference.

Although the First Committee encountered setbacks in the work of the naval conference due to Japan's withdrawal, it was still able to make progress. The parties to the naval conference expressed satisfaction with this today. The committee unanimously passed an important proposal on exchanging shipbuilding procedures. It is the consensus that this is a good sign for the smooth progress of its future work. People who are very close to the representatives of various countries now hold a kind of hope that when the First Committee continues to meet tomorrow, it will be able to agree on the general instructions to be given to the technical sub-committee. Then, the sub-committee will discuss everything in order to draft a full text of an agreement. Once the sub-committee passes the issue, the First Committee will discuss the issue of qualitative disarmament. All newspapers are now emphasizing the importance of stipulating clauses to prevent competition in the types of warships, as this could lead to naval competition in a dangerous way. However, several parties now believe that the committee will be able to reach a compromise on the main points of the whole issue. It is expected that if the Four-Power Conference can once agree on a temporary agreement on exchanging shipbuilding procedures and qualitative naval disarmament, it will invite other naval countries that have not sent representatives to the naval conference to send representatives to freely discuss the results achieved with the four countries. Any agreement will of course contain a safeguard clause, so that signatory countries may declare the cancellation of the agreement if the actions of non-signatory countries force them to declare its cancellation.

Inviting Japan to Send Observers 55

The committee passed a letter to Nagano, the chief Japanese representative, stating that it was regrettable that the Japanese side had decided to withdraw from the conference, and asking him to continue to participate in the conference as an observer. The meeting was then adjourned until tomorrow, at which time a small committee will be appointed to summarize the plans opened by Britain, France, and Italy for discussing qualitative restrictions. (Reuters, 16th)

London The representatives of Britain, the United States, France, and Italy attending the London Naval Conference today invited the Japanese representatives who withdrew from the conference yesterday to send observers to participate in the remaining discussions, but the Japanese representatives may not attend a special committee where the representatives of the four countries will discuss their procedures. (National Telegram, 16th)

The Status of the Naval Conference Remains Unchanged 56

The committee also agreed that the status of the naval conference should not be changed in the slightest, and should still be called the 1935 London Naval Conference. A British representative explained to a Reuters reporter the reason for not changing the status of the conference, saying that it was hoped that the various resolutions of the naval conference would be accepted by Japan in the future, as the usefulness and merit of the various resolutions depended largely on Japan's attitude towards the resolutions. He deeply regretted Japan's withdrawal from the conference, and if the Japanese side had not been so resolute, the naval conference could have accomplished good work. Japanese newspapers claim that Japan does not want to embark on a warship competition. This is true, and other countries do not want this competition either. But without a compromise, I am afraid that competition will be unavoidable. The most dangerous competition is in the qualitative aspect. Britain sympathizes with Japan's political difficulties, but Japan's withdrawal from the conference, its unwillingness to discuss quantitative or qualitative restrictions, and its unwillingness to exchange shipbuilding procedures, only makes the crisis of competition more urgent.

Britain and the United States Will Not Compete in Shipbuilding 57

When a Reuters reporter asked whether there was a possibility of shipbuilding competition between Britain and the United States, the speaker replied that the two countries had the same purpose and both wanted to maintain the principle of equality, but there was no agreement to bind both parties. Judging from this, the United States does not seem to recognize the need to increase the strength of cruisers. The speaker also said that the British and American representatives did not want to have bilateral talks on the issue of relative numbers. It has been found that Britain and the United States had bilateral talks long before the naval conference closed. Judging from the British spokesperson's remarks now, both parties have already had a satisfactory and clear understanding on this point. (Reuters, 16th)

The Naval Conference Continues to Meet 58

London According to the naval conference, this reporter learned from British official circles that the delegations of the four countries to the naval conference are scheduled to discuss tomorrow the suggestions made by France, Italy, and Britain regarding the exchange of shipbuilding information, so as to establish an agreement in principle, and then appoint several experts to form a sub-committee to stipulate the details of the implementation of the above suggestions. At the same time, the naval conference will discuss the general issue of qualitative restrictions. It is generally believed that there is considerable hope of reaching an agreement on this matter. As for the invitation of the Soviet Union and Russia to participate in the conference, it will be considered only after the above-mentioned agreement in principle has been established. In the future, observers from Japan will attend the meetings of the General Committee of the Naval Conference. Once an agreement is reached, Japan will also be notified of its contents. The British side advocates that the nature of the agreement must be as general as possible, and must also include a guarantee clause to cope with the various needs arising from Japan's future naval policy. (Havas News Agency, 16th)

London The spokesperson for the British delegation issued a statement on the 16th, saying that the First Committee decided at its meeting on the 16th to continue the 1935 London Disarmament Conference, the purpose of which is to enable Japan to participate in the repatriation agreement in the future. Japan's participation in the agreement is of great importance to the effectiveness of the naval agreement. Therefore, any treaties concluded by the four countries must adopt a form in which Japan can participate, because Britain sincerely hopes that Japan will ease its attitude in the future and participate in the agreement. It is a pity that Japan suddenly announced its withdrawal when the conference was about to discuss the issue of quality. If Japan's attitude had some accommodating nature, such a situation could have been avoided. Japan has made it clear that it has no intention of competing in shipbuilding, but if there is no similar agreement on restrictions, competition is almost inevitable. In this case, the only effective limitation on capacity is the limit of each country's financial capacity. However, this financial restriction is by no means a sufficient restriction, and competition in the qualitative aspect is more dangerous. It is a pity that Japan withdrew from the conference before we discussed the issue of quantitative and qualitative restrictions. The revision of the Washington Treaty has lost hope due to Japan's withdrawal from the conference. Today, Britain must also re-examine the issue of Pacific defense. (Domei News Agency, 16th)

Roman Newspaper Comments 59

The Roman evening newspapers today criticized Japan's withdrawal from the London Naval Conference, all agreeing that Japan's move has clarified the situation of the naval issue, because all international conferences are nothing but beneficial to the strongest countries, who set specific disadvantageous ratios for other countries, thinking that it is convenient for themselves. There is nothing more hateful than this. The naval conference is also the same. Moreover, since the conclusion of the Washington Treaty, competition among countries in shipbuilding within limits has become a competition for political advantages. Therefore, from our observation, Japan's withdrawal from the naval conference is not a disaster. On the contrary, the situation in which countries were at odds and were constantly arguing has now disappeared, and Japan can build the navy it wants as it pleases according to its needs. The Badano Post said that those who want to engage in negotiations will find that their dreams are in vain, because negotiations will ultimately only involve the necessary objectives. (Havas News Agency, 16th)

The Japanese Delegation Prepares to Pack Up and Return Home 60

London Nagano and Nagai, the two plenipotentiaries, and other members of the Japanese delegation, are scheduled to leave England on the 24th on the Japanese postal ship Hakone Maru and return to their country, requesting government permission. (Domei News Agency, 16th)

Comparison of Naval Power Among Britain, the United States, and Japan 61

Tokyo Due to the breakdown of the arms reduction conference, the Japanese Navy is watching the attitudes of Britain and the United States with a cautious attitude, as there will be no treaty to limit the military preparations of various countries. The current actual strength of Britain, the United States, and Japan, that is, the total tonnage of warships, is 700,000 tons for Japan, 800,000 tons for the United States, and 1,000,000 tons for Britain. The difference between Japan and the United States is only 100,000 tons. Comparing only auxiliary ships, Japan has 350,000 tons, the United States has 270,000 tons, and Britain has 390,000 tons. However, since 1931, the United States has been carrying out shipbuilding work with the Benson Plan and the industrial recovery funds, building a navy within the scope allowed by the treaty. When this plan is completed, that is, in 1941, the actual ratio between Japan and the United States will become 6 to 10, with Japan occupying a 60% disadvantage in naval power against the United States. Therefore, the Japanese Navy has decided on a policy to establish an independent economic military preparation for the completion of national defense in these few years. Observing the shipbuilding status of Britain and the United States, and anticipating the future status, they hold the view that there will not be fierce shipbuilding competition.

"United States" Since 1931, the United States has started the construction of 61 warships in total, including those under construction and those planned for construction in the future, with a total tonnage of 229,000 tons. However, because its 15 capital ships have exceeded the prescribed number of years of service, they will have to start building new ships to replace them next year when the treaty expires. Therefore, judging from its capacity, it is definitely unable to expand its shipbuilding plan beyond the established plan. Moreover, judging from the domestic situation, it does not seem likely to start building large warships immediately.

"Britain" Since 1931, Britain has built three Class B cruisers, nine destroyers, and three submarines every year, and has also implemented a major plan to supplement auxiliary ships. However, many of Britain's capital ships are old and will need to build three ships in 1941 and eight ships in 1942. As for its aircraft carriers, except for the Hermes, all are old ships and are busy building their replacements. (Domei News Agency, 17th)

London The Daily Telegraph recently learned that the naval shipbuilding program recently formulated by the Cabinet Defense Committee stipulates that all types of warships must be started to be built to reach the limits permitted by the Washington and London Treaties. As for the cruiser item, the London Treaty stipulates a limit of 50 vessels, and it is now planned to build 70 vessels immediately. (Note: Britain has long advocated increasing the number of cruisers to 70. (Havas News Agency, 17th)

London The Morning Post, with the authorization of the authorities, began today to publicize the Cabinet's policy of consolidating military preparations in a major way. Most dignitaries, such as the Archbishop of York, Admiral of the Navy Lord Beatty, former Ambassador to France Lord Tyrrell, former Foreign Secretary Austen Chamberlain, and Zhang Bolun, have all sent letters to the newspaper to support this policy. In addition, the newspaper also published an article exposing the weaknesses of the British Navy. It is said that after several British warships were sent to the Mediterranean last year, well-informed people in the naval circles immediately realized that once these warships seriously engaged in combat and used ammunition, the ammunition would be exhausted after one battle. This is one of the weaknesses. From 1927 to 1932, the number of naval personnel was repeatedly reduced, resulting in a lack of experienced soldiers in the British Navy. This is the second weakness. Regarding this point, the newspaper advocates that naval soldiers whose terms of service have expired should continue to serve. Also, the number of capital ships, cruisers, and destroyers in Britain is insufficient, and the construction of new ships is too slow. For example, only three armored ships can be built at the same time. This is the third weakness. (Havas News Agency, 17th)

Foreign Affairs Councilor Sir Vansittart, Chief of Naval Staff Admiral Chatfield, and Chief of Air Staff General Ellington all attended. According to this reporter, the British Cabinet is now most concerned about the issue of consolidating military preparations, because if the League of Nations wants to implement a tough policy, it must be supported by effective methods. In addition, Germany is now actively reorganizing its military preparations, and it is said that its scale is extremely large, which has made the Cabinet uneasy. Therefore, it is planned to issue new national defense bonds to fund the consolidation of military preparations. According to financial circles, the Army Department recently contacted the famous arms dealer Vickers-Armstrong Factory to order arms, and it is said that the quantity is more than four times the factory's existing manufacturing capacity. It is also said that Rolls-Royce, which specializes in manufacturing automobile and aircraft engines, has also been requested by the government to reduce automobile production in order to increase the production of aircraft engines. The authorities are now planning to explain the various needs of the diplomatic situation to public opinion, and to persuade them to accept a large-scale plan for consolidating military preparations. The Morning Post has been authorized by the government to start this publicity today. It is heard that the Cabinet anticipates that Germany will raise issues such as abolishing the demilitarized zone on both sides of the Rhine River, Austria, Memel, and colonies, so the above-mentioned plan for consolidating military preparations is eagerly hoped to be completed in advance in preparation for it. Regarding the colonial issue, the Cabinet generally intends to avoid the use of force and supports amending the current colonial system in a peaceful manner in accordance with Article 19 of the Covenant of the League of Nations. (Havas News Agency, 16th)

New Weapons Fiercely Attack the Southern Route, Italian Forces Report Victory, Advancing Over Forty Miles in Four Days 67

A correspondent with the Italian army reports today from Rome about the fierce battle between the main force of the Abyssinian army under General Nasibu and the Italian column under General Graziani near the Ganale Dorya River. The report states that the battle has virtually ended, with the Italian forces advancing over 43 miles in four days. The Italian forces faced fierce resistance from machine-gun nests hidden in camouflaged semi-circular trenches. However, Italian tanks drove to the edge of the trenches and bombarded the defenders with machine guns, capturing the position. One of the most notable events in the battle was an Abyssinian cavalry charge against Italian troops advancing along the south bank of the river. Italian tanks rushed to their aid, and although the Abyssinian troops fought to the death, they were ultimately mowed down by the tanks' machine guns. At the same time, Italian aircraft bombed the Abyssinian army's rear formations to prevent reinforcements, and also bombed Nasibu's headquarters, though it is not yet known if they scored a direct hit. This battle is seen as a prelude to a major Italian victory. (Reuters dispatch, 16th)

It is learned here in Rome today that General Graziani's forces intend to make a final effort before the rainy season arrives, seeking to avenge the recent Italian losses in Abyssinia. They continue to attack the native troops on the southern front, inflicting 2,000 casualties on the enemy. Observers here believe that Graziani's objective is the Djibouti railway, hoping to disrupt its traffic. (National News Agency dispatch, 16th)

Italy's Economic Situation, Italian Newspapers Claim Currency Value Stable, Unaffected by League of Nations Sanctions 69

Today marks the sixtieth day since the implementation of economic sanctions in Rome. Italian newspapers take this opportunity to publish a report on the economic situation over the past two months. The press claims that the most significant phenomenon in Italy since the implementation of economic sanctions two months ago is the stability of currency and prices. Generally speaking, food prices have not risen at all. Price stability is a sign of currency stability, and currency stability is a sign of purchasing power. This situation also benefits Italy's foreign exchange considerably. According to exchange rates, the Italian currency has not depreciated in major markets such as London and New York. (National News Agency dispatch, 16th)

Three Sources of War Expenses Against Abyssinia 70

The semi-official Italian newspaper, Il Popolo d'Italia, recently reported that the budget expenditure for the fiscal year 1936-1937 does not include any item for war expenses against Abyssinia. All war expenses are derived from the following three sources: issuing treasury bonds; converting old government bonds with higher interest rates into new 5% government bonds; forcibly converting foreign securities and Italian securities issued abroad into Italian bonds or new treasury bills. From this perspective, the expenses of the East African war are purely funded by special treasury funds, and no additional taxes or levies have been imposed to increase the burden on the people. (Havas News Agency dispatch, 17th)

Laval Unsettled as French Chamber of Deputies Meets, Herriot Resolves to Resign from Cabinet 73

Paris When the French Chamber of Deputies met today, the left-wing parties opposed Prime Minister Laval's request for an immediate discussion of agricultural policy. Laval treated this as a matter of confidence and put it to a vote, which he passed with 315 votes to 251. After the adjournment, Herriot, a cabinet member without portfolio, decided to resign from the cabinet on Saturday because his Radical Socialist Party was at odds with the government. Upon hearing this news, Laval said that if other Radical Socialist cabinet members also resigned, he himself would consider resigning. However, in any case, he would still go to Geneva on Sunday to attend the League of Nations Executive Council meeting. During today's meeting of the Chamber of Deputies, a speaker from an independent socialist party criticized Laval's foreign policy, saying that Laval's advocacy of simultaneously allying with Great Britain, Italy, and Russia would achieve nothing. The speaker wanted the government to clearly announce its foreign policy before the general election and Laval's trip to Geneva. Laval replied that the Chamber of Deputies had already approved the government's foreign policy, so there was no need for this. (Reuters dispatch, 16th)

Japanese Parliament Reconvenes on the 21st, Foreign Minister Hirota's Policy Speech Highlights, Confirming Sino-Japanese Relations Will Proceed Based on Three Principles, Demanding Soviet Russian Army Withdrawal 76

Tokyo Foreign Minister Hirota will make a statement on foreign policy to China and foreign countries on the day the parliament reconvenes on the 21st. This will be Japan's first expression of foreign policy after the breakdown of the naval conference, and it will also clarify its policy toward China before the Sino-Japanese Nanjing Conference is convened, attracting much attention from all sides. The main points of the Foreign Minister's speech are roughly as follows:

Japan is the only stabilizing force in East Asia, maintaining an important position, which has gradually been recognized by various countries. The people should be determined to maintain this force and establish its position.

Relations between Japan and Manchukuo: The political and economic relations between Japan and Manchukuo are becoming closer and stronger due to the sound development of Manchukuo. Japan, in order to promote the development of Manchukuo, demands the adjustment of Sino-Japanese and Japanese-Russian relations.

Sino-Japanese Relations: There is no other way to establish friendly Sino-Japanese relations except to implement the three principles proposed by Japan. China has already acknowledged these three principles, which is most gratifying.

(According to a Dentsu News Agency dispatch, the three principles are: (A) China should eliminate its anti-Japanese attitude and genuinely strive for peace in East Asia, in which case Japan is prepared to assist China in seeking stability in East Asia; (B) improve Sino-Japanese-Manchukuo relations centered on North China; (C) prevent the Red movement, which is a major obstacle to peace in East Asia, etc.)

Japanese-Russian Relations: Japanese-Russian relations centered on Manchukuo have been further improved with the conclusion of the Sino-Eastern Railway sales agreement. However, regrettable disputes have repeatedly occurred on the Russian-Manchukuo border. The Japanese government, in order to adjust Japanese-Russian relations, is striving to resolve various outstanding issues between the two countries and believes that the withdrawal of the Far Eastern Red Army is the most effective measure and intends to negotiate this matter with the Russian side.

Naval Disarmament Conference: After the breakdown of the conference, the Japanese government continued to strive to maintain friendly relations with various countries. Japan firmly believes that the fundamental policy of the Japanese government will be approved by various countries in the future, thereby contributing to the establishment of world peace. (Domei News Agency dispatch, 17th)

Lindbergh Kidnapping Case, Criminal Granted 30-Day Reprieve, Authorized by New Jersey Governor 80

Trenton, USA Bruno Hauptmann, the criminal who kidnapped and murdered Colonel Lindbergh's young son, has been sentenced to death and was originally scheduled to be executed on Friday night. Today, New Jersey Governor Hoffman granted a 30-day reprieve in order to study new evidence. The governor's motive for granting the reprieve was not announced, but it is clearly due to new evidence or a new witness. The governor said, "Legally speaking, there are many reasons why I granted the reprieve. Personally, I have no doubt about Ho's guilt, but in the minds of millions of people, there are still doubts." The governor added that he currently has no intention of granting another reprieve. When he announced the reprieve, Attorney General Wilentz issued an opinion, saying that the governor had no such power because more than 90 days had passed since the verdict against Ho. The governor said that there were precedents for this matter, but once the news was released, there was a great deal of criticism from the outside. American Antarctic Explorers Safe 82

Sydney American explorer Ellsworth and Kenyon set off from Dundee Island on November 23 last year, intending to fly 2,000 miles across the Southern Ocean to Little America, and then went missing. A short telegram was received here today, stating that the exploration ship had discovered a reconnaissance aircraft No. 2, which had seen Ellsworth's aircraft when flying over Whale Bay, and had also seen one person. A rescue plane has now been dispatched to rescue this person, but it was not mentioned whether this person was Ellsworth or his companion Kenyon. (Reuters dispatch, 17th)

London The Colonial Office received a telegram from the exploration ship No. 2 today, stating that Ellsworth and his companion Kenyon were both safe and sound. News of Ellsworth and his companion's survival was received here yesterday, but due to bad weather, many of the radio messages were garbled. Experts speculate that the aircraft No. 2 discovered the missing aircraft yesterday, but returned to the ship to report due to the fading daylight. This morning, they returned to the area and rescued Ellsworth and his companion. A subsequent telegram stated that a telegram received here this afternoon stated that aircraft No. 2 initially saw the missing aircraft 5 miles from Little America, and circled around for a long time before seeing Kenyon emerge from the aircraft. They dropped food and letters and flew back to report. Soon after, the ship dispatched a team to rescue Kenyon and bring him on board. According to Kenyon, Ellsworth is alive and well, but is suffering from a slight cold. The rescue team is continuing to advance to find him. Kenyon also said that the aircraft they were flying ran out of gasoline 20 miles from Little America and was forced to land. (Reuters dispatch, 17th)

Reuters Special Commercial Report, January 17

Gold and Silver

British Gold: The London premium rose one penny today to 140 shillings and 11 pence.

British Silver: As expected, the London silver market rose .875 today to 19 pence. Speculators sold unanimously, but there were very few buyers. The market was stable when prices fell. Tomorrow is the settlement date for Bombay, so the position of the silver market is now approaching the final stage. The opening chips in London gradually decreased, but are estimated to be around 10 million ounces, so there is a need to replenish spot sales.

American Silver: The London silver price fell, so the Mount Airy silver market also fell accordingly at the opening. The March price was 42.00 to 50, which was 100 pounds lower than yesterday's closing price.

Exchange Rates

British-American: The London foreign exchange market was quiet this morning, with very little price fluctuation. The British-American exchange rate was 4.955625 at 10:30 a.m., which was .1875 lower than yesterday's closing price for American-British, but then rose .125 to 4.956875. This price did not change until 1:00 p.m.

Cotton and Wheat

American Cotton: The New York cotton market opened steadily because it was heard that the representatives of the cotton-producing states had obtained the government's permission to not cancel the cotton subsidy plan that stipulates a price of 12 cents per pound. On the other hand, merchants were quite worried, feeling that the new cotton production control law would be difficult to establish based on the constitution. The opening price did not move, and then the price rose due to buying activity.

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market opened slightly lower due to long liquidation, and the market was quite apprehensive because people believed that the new cotton production control procedure under the American Agricultural Adjustment Act would be difficult to implement under the constitution.

British Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market opened steadily, expressing sympathy for overseas markets and because the shipping quantity was too small. At 1:00 p.m., the March price rose .75 to 6 shillings and 8.125 pence.

American Wheat: The Chicago wheat market was quiet because merchants were waiting quietly for developments in Washington. The May delivery fell .25 at the opening, and feed grains rose slightly. The opening price for May delivery was 60.125.

New York: The New York rubber market was quiet this morning. The opening fell 4 pounds due to long liquidation. Trading was not very active.

Guangdong Students' Patriotic Movement: Guangzhou Declares Martial Law; Students' Parade in Lychee Bay Clashes with Anti-Traitors Corps; Primary Schools Also Affected, Temporarily Suspending Classes for One Week 88

Guangzhou Correspondence: The student patriotic demonstration movement in Guangdong Province is expanding daily. Students from Zhongshan University are dispatching teams to various schools in the city to coordinate unified action, planning to suspend classes and embark on promotional activities. Two student demonstrations have already been discovered in Guangzhou. On the 13th of this month, a clash and brawl occurred between students and the Patriotic Anti-Traitors Corps in Lychee Bay. The details are as follows:

Lychee Bay Incident

Students from Guangzhou National University held a meeting at their school in Lychee Bay on the morning of the 13th, resolving to: immediately go on strike; request the school to waive the semester exams and grant everyone a passing grade; request the school to provide a promotional allowance of 200 yuan. After the meeting, undergraduates and affiliated high school students from Zhongshan University, along with students from the Municipal Second High School, arrived at the scene, joining the National University students in a parade. At that time, about 500 to 600 male and female students from various schools lined up and proceeded along Duobao Road from the National University playground. As the student procession crossed the Lychee Bay Bridge, a car suddenly approached, stopping abruptly at the side of the bridge. Over a dozen people in plain clothes got out of the car. One of them held a banner of the "Guangzhou Citizens' Anti-Traitors Corps" and rushed forward to explain something to the parading students. In the course of the conversation, a conflict arose. The two sides exchanged blows, and the order was disrupted for a time. Some students were squeezed and injured. The dispute lasted for forty to fifty minutes before the military police arrived to suppress it, and order was restored. Not long after, more than 200 students went to Xicun, intending to contact students from the Provincial Guangya Middle School. Before they reached the school gate, the second squadron of the school's volunteer corps was stationed inside. Upon seeing the students, they stepped forward to dissuade them. Fortunately, no further conflict occurred. Upon receiving the report, the authorities, fearing further incidents due to the continuous student demonstrations, declared a temporary martial law in Guangzhou City from noon on the 13th. The entire city was divided into four districts for management: 1. The Yantang and Shahe area was the responsibility of the Military and Political School. 2. The Henan and Dongshan area was the responsibility of the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau. 3. The Xiaobei, Sh Pai, Huangsha, and Xicun area was the responsibility of the Training Division. 4. Dongshan, Henan, and the city proper were defended by the Public Security Bureau's Security Team.

Students' Petition

After the Lychee Bay incident, a large group of students went to the Political Affairs Committee to petition. Chen Jitang and Zou Lu were present at the time and met with student representatives. In addition to reporting the events of the Lychee Bay incident, the student representatives also petitioned the Political Affairs Committee to: release the arrested students; punish the perpetrators who beat the students; and ensure the safety of students in the future. Chen and others promised to investigate the truth before taking action.

University President Resigns

In this expanded student patriotic demonstration movement, the students and faculty of Zhongshan University were the most enthusiastic. Unfortunately, an accident occurred. On the 13th, Zhong Da President Zou Lu sent another telegram requesting dismissal. At the same time, Fan Qi, Dean of the Faculty of Arts, Zheng Yanfen, Dean of the Faculty of Law, Xiao Guanying, Dean of the Faculty of Engineering, Deng Zhiyi, Dean of the Faculty of Agriculture, and Liu Zuxia, Dean of the Faculty of Medicine, jointly requested the university president to resign from the concurrent position of dean, citing that the student patriotic movement had gone beyond the proper boundaries, and that the deans had failed in their leadership.

Primary School Suspension

Students from secondary and higher schools have mostly suspended classes in recent days to engage in patriotic movements. Fearing that the city's public and private primary schools would be affected, they temporarily suspended classes for one week starting on the 14th, allowing primary school students to review at home in preparation for the semester exams upon resumption. A letter was also sent to the parents of primary school students, restricting them from going out during the suspension period.

Organizing Volunteer Corps

Since the authorities ordered the organization of the Patriotic Volunteer Corps, the captains of each corps (the dispatch of the general captain and three squadron leaders has been reported previously) took office on the 11th. On the same day, the corps headquarters was established, and a notice was issued to start registration. An independent squadron was also established, with Huang Bao appointed as the independent squadron leader. The independent squadron headquarters was set up at the old campus of Zhongshan University on Wenming Road. In addition, the General Headquarters dispatched five major service members to serve at the Volunteer Corps General Headquarters, taking charge of the work. However, in recent days, very few students have registered. According to the general captain, if students are enthusiastic about saving the country, they can register at each corps headquarters at any time to wait for training. If they do not serve, they can attend classes as usual. The organization of the Volunteer Corps is the same as that of the infantry, with four squadrons forming a battalion, and each squadron is set at ninety people (i.e., a company of ordinary infantry). The first step is to engage in unarmed training, and the second step is to issue military equipment for practice by the General Headquarters. The organizational regulations of the Volunteer Corps are as follows: To abide by the Southwest Political Affairs Committee's organization of the Guangdong Patriotic Volunteer Corps, specific organizational regulations are formulated for compliance. The Patriotic Volunteer Corps is composed of male and female students and faculty who are enthusiastic about saving the country. The soldiers of the Patriotic Volunteer Corps are composed of men, who are given strict military training and various combat exercises to cultivate the habits of hard work, endurance, and obedience. Women are organized into nursing teams, which are given appropriate military training and various battlefield rescue exercises, with the main emphasis on practicality. The Patriotic Volunteer Corps has a General Headquarters, with several battalions and squads under it, organized in the order of first, second, and third class. Officers at all levels are appointed or concurrently held by the Commander-in-Chief of the First Army Group. All school faculty and students who are genuinely enthusiastic about saving the country and willing to join the corps for training can register with each corps headquarters and wait for assignment. Soldiers are issued a monthly food allowance of six yuan, which is provided by the original school. Soldiers should abide by the same discipline as the military. Those who violate laws and regulations will be punished according to military law. These regulations will be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Shanxi Province Establishes a Goods Reserve Depository to Purchase Agricultural Products and Aid Farmers and Workers; All Industries in the City Are Also Extremely Depressed 89

Taiyuan Correspondence: Since the implementation of the legal tender policy in Shanxi Province, there have been no special changes in market prices. Regarding social finance, since the political changes in the 19th year of the Republic, Shanxi banknotes have plummeted, causing significant losses to the people, and their vitality has not yet recovered. In recent years, although efforts have been made to maintain the surface, the actual situation has been in a state of irreversible decline for a long time. Recently, the authorities have advocated the establishment of public land villages and the implementation of two major new policies of property securities. The future advantages and disadvantages of these new policies cannot be predicted. However, when these matters were advocated but not yet implemented, the people in various counties were indeed unable to borrow money and had no way out, finding themselves in a desperate situation. Most of the people usually regard land as a treasure for making a living, which can be cultivated to support themselves and can also be used to exchange goods. Most of the loans in rural areas are secured by land. Recently, after the method of returning land to public villages was spread, it coincided with the implementation of the legal tender policy. As a result, the current silver dollars that originally circulated were all hidden. The inherent ability of social economic activities had already lost most of its function. At the same time, land was no longer valued by people, and they held the idea that it would not belong to them. As a result, the economic situation of the people immediately showed a stagnant phenomenon. No one would lend money, regardless of the interest rate. Items worth hundreds of yuan, when pawned, even if you want to pawn one-tenth or one-twelfth of their value, are often rejected. The poor situation in various counties, although not unprecedented, is indeed unparalleled. Recognizing this, the authorities, in order to quickly raise relief, ordered the four banks publicly operated by the Shanxi Provincial Bank—the Sui-Xi Reclamation Bank, the Railway Bank, and the Salt Industry Bank—to jointly establish a "Goods Fully Prepared Depository." The four banks jointly raised funds to organize its establishment, purchasing as much folk agricultural and industrial products as possible for turnover. After many days of preparation, the depository officially started operating on New Year's Day this year, immediately sending staff to various counties, starting with the purchase of agricultural products. In the future, other items will be collected one by one. It is heard that in a few days, the amount of cotton and wheat collected has reached three to four million yuan, so grain prices have begun to rebound, and merchants and people also have a slight hope of escaping poverty. However, a distant source cannot quench a present thirst. Within the New Year, it is feared that the various counties in the province will not be able to universally benefit, which is regrettable. Yan Xishan personally serves as the general manager of the depository, and the funds are unlimited. It is predetermined that if there are certain goods and how much the demand for the goods is, the four banks will allocate that much. The provincial bank is responsible for 50% of the investment, the Railway Bank is responsible for 35%, the Reclamation Bank is responsible for 10%, and the Salt Industry Bank is responsible for 5%. Although these funds are all banknotes currently in use by the respective banks, the general merchants and people still consider it reasonable to have real goods as reserves. After the depository purchased a large number of agricultural products in recent days, grain prices suddenly rose. In order to balance the situation, the authorities telegraphed to the various branch depositories to sell at the original price, only increasing the handling fee by one-quarter of 35 per mille of the original price for expenses. They also plan to use the collected wheat to grind flour and sell it at a low price, and they are currently discussing machinery matters with the Jinfeng Flour Company and various flour mills.

The rules and contents of the Goods Fully Prepared Depository are as follows:

(Article 1) These rules are formulated in accordance with the provisions of Article 6 of the Provisional Regulations of this Depository, and are named the Shanxi Provincial Bank, Jinsui Local Railway Bank, Suixi Reclamation Bank, and Jinbei Salt Industry Bank Goods Fully Prepared Depository (hereinafter referred to as the Goods Prepared Depository). (Article 2) This Depository is located in the provincial capital of Shanxi. When necessary, it may request the approval of the Taiyuan Economic Construction Committee (hereinafter referred to as the Economic Committee) to set up branch depositories in other counties. Its organization shall be temporarily submitted for approval. (Article 3) In accordance with the provisions of Article 3 of the Provisional Regulations, this Depository establishes commercial firms or entrusts commercial firms to receive various properties from the people. The required funds are borne by the Shanxi Provincial Bank for 50%, the Jinsui Local Railway Bank for 35%, the Suixi Reclamation Bank for 10%, and the Jinbei Salt Industry Bank for 5%. The aforementioned funds should be given to each bank by the depository at 2% of the issuance cost annually. (Article 4) The four banks that provide funds should jointly form an audit institution to audit the accounting and warehouses of the Goods Prepared Depository. If it is necessary to restrict the acceptance of the people's properties, it may also be restricted with the permission of the Economic Committee. (Article 5) This Depository has one manager, who manages the affairs of the Depository, and two assistant managers, who assist the manager in handling the Depository's affairs, and are selected and sent by the Economic Committee. When the manager is unable to perform his duties due to an event, the Economic Committee designates one of the assistant managers to act on his behalf. (Article 6) The following matters should be drafted by the manager and assistant managers and submitted to the Economic Committee for approval: business policy, establishment and revocation of branch depositories, expenses and other important expenditures, internal regulations, and other matters that should be requested for instructions. (Article 7) This Depository has the following groups: the Administrative Group and the Business Group. Each group has one group leader and one deputy group leader, and several group members and clerks, who are selected and appointed by the managers and assistant managers to handle the affairs under their jurisdiction. (Article 8) The affairs under the jurisdiction of the Administrative Group are as follows: matters concerning drafting regulations, drafting documents, receiving and sending documents, and keeping files; matters concerning keeping seals and stamps; matters concerning general affairs; matters concerning receiving and paying money; matters concerning the preparation, registration, and keeping of various account books and forms; matters concerning auditing all accounting matters of commercial firms or agent commercial firms; and other matters not belonging to the business. (Article 9) The affairs under the jurisdiction of the Business Group are as follows: matters concerning accepting the people's properties and selling the inventory; matters concerning the appraisal and safekeeping of physical samples; matters concerning the appraisal of physical prices; matters concerning the inspection of physical objects; matters concerning the determination of commissions; matters concerning the safekeeping and transportation of goods; matters concerning the safekeeping of all contracts and evidences. (Article 10) The expenses of this Depository should be budgeted and submitted to the Economic Committee for approval in accordance with the provisions of Article 7 of the Provisional Regulations. (Article 11) This Depository shall settle once in June and December each year, and the annual final accounts shall be prepared with the following books and tables and submitted to the Economic Committee for verification: balance sheet, property catalog, profit and loss statement, business report. (Article 12) If there is a loss after the final settlement of this Depository, it shall be compensated by the Economic Committee. (Article 13) The business situation of this Depository shall be investigated and announced to all counties by seven supervisors representing merchants and people in the province every month. (Article 14) These rules shall be implemented from the date of distribution by the Taiyuan Economic Construction Committee.

The difficult situation in the counties is as described above, and the provincial capital of Taiyuan is also difficult to escape from this exception. Before the solar calendar New Year, officials and businessmen worked hard to maintain it. The Provincial Bank and other four banks borrowed hundreds of thousands of yuan from money shops to get through the standard year. However, now it is approaching the abandoned Lunar New Year, and various commercial firms still feel it difficult to cope. Recently, the Municipal General Chamber of Commerce, at the request of the 22 guilds of various industries, submitted a request to the two Provincial Offices, requesting the official authorities to establish a real estate mortgage bank. After receiving the report, the two offices are currently studying the method. The original report of the Municipal General Chamber of Commerce is as follows: "According to the chairmen of various guilds, since the currency reform, the current silver dollars in the city have been checked and sealed and cannot be used. However, the banknotes issued by the four major banks in the province, which are currently circulating in the market, are not sufficient for turnover. At this time of financial stagnation and commercial depression, the old Lunar New Year is approaching. If no measures are taken to relieve the situation, large and small commercial firms will inevitably collapse, and the impact on the market and local security will be significant. The Ministry of Finance is planning to establish a real estate mortgage lending bank and revise the real estate mortgage laws and regulations to revitalize the locality. It is proposed to imitate this meaning, and where merchants and people have real estate to mortgage for loans, they should be allowed to borrow from the four major banks at 50% of the market price of the property at that time, and issue the loan at a small profit, and return it on a regular basis. If this is done, the market can be slightly expected to be active, and not only will commerce be maintained, but real estate can be expected to be revitalized, and the four major banks can also receive a stable profit with real real estate as collateral. This is a triple benefit. The chamber is a representative of merchants and people, and does not dare to remain silent, so we report the situation in particular. If you are pleased to approve it, we implore you to order the four major banks to properly formulate measures and announce them for compliance, which is a virtue. All the reasons for the petition to the four major banks to establish a real estate mortgage lending are that we have something to do, and we should submit a document and ask for your approval and compliance. Respectfully presented by Taiyuan Pacification Director Yan, Shanxi Provincial Government Chairman Xu, and Taiyuan Municipal General Chamber of Commerce Chairman Wang Zhaotai." In the midst of the people's poverty and the exhaustion of wealth, and the decline of all industries, the results of the money industry's account settlement for the 24th year show a considerable surplus. The business conditions of the various silver money industries in the city in the 24th year, as investigated by the Municipal General Chamber of Commerce, are as follows: (1) The Provincial Bank's net profit was 400,000 yuan. (2) The Railway Bank's net profit was 600,000 yuan. (3) The Reclamation Bank's net profit was 50,000 yuan. (4) The Salt Industry Bank's net profit was more than 30,000 yuan. (5) The Hehesheng's net profit was more than 3,000 yuan. (6) The Xinghua Bank's net profit was more than 6,000 yuan. (7) The Jinyu Bank's net profit was 50,000 yuan. (8) The Jinxing Money Shop's net profit was 70,000 yuan. (9) The Renfagong's net profit was 120,000 yuan. (10) The Dexingchang's net profit was 5,000 yuan. (11) The Tongxiang Bank's net profit was 3,000 yuan. (12) The Yuanshengli's net profit was 11,000 yuan. (13) The Jinyi Bank's net profit was more than 6,000 yuan. The Ministry of Finance Replies to the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce: The Government is Determined to Consolidate Credit and is Planning Everything Carefully for Economic Recovery, Hoping to Sincerely Inform Merchants and People to Share This Intention and Not to be Exploited by Speculators, Causing Self-Alarm 93

Central News Agency, Nanjing, 17th: After receiving the telegram from the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce on the 15th, the Ministry of Finance replied to the Chamber on the 17th. The government's efforts to consolidate credit have long been known to the world. In recent years, the national crisis has been severe, banditry has spread, rivers have flooded, and disasters have spread throughout the country. Moreover, it has been affected by the fluctuations of the global economic panic and the rise in silver prices, resulting in rural decay, industrial and commercial stagnation, financial exhaustion, and the depression of all industries. Therefore, the Ministry declared on November 4 last year that, regarding the major issues of improving the financial system, developing production, reducing imports, and balancing income and expenditure, the government will carefully plan everything that is beneficial to the people and is a necessary path for economic recovery, in order to meet the needs of the times, carefully consider, and selectively implement to strengthen the country's foundation and benefit the people's livelihood. If you frequently request the government to express its views, it will not only be too much trouble, but it will actually be exploited by speculators. At this time when people's hearts are uncertain, you should not be tempted by those who seek temporary and selfish gains, causing self-alarm. Seal of Kong Shao, Minister of Finance."

The Issue of Various Shops Collecting Designated Banknotes Has Been Mediated and Resolved; However, Negotiations Are Still Underway with the Dalu and Donglai Banks; The Two-Year Term for Collecting Legal Tender is Canceled for Repurchase 94

New Voice News: Since the Ministry of Finance stipulated on November 4 last year that the banknotes of the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications would be legal tender, various issuing banks canceled the method of collecting designated banknotes, causing opposition from the collectors. Now, except for the Dalu Bank and the Donglai Bank, the rest have been resolved. The details are as follows:

Centralized Issuance and Cancellation of Designated Banknotes

Various money shops and banks have a method of collecting designated banknotes, using 60% cash and 40% guarantee to collect designated banknotes, or using 100% cash to collect designated banknotes. However, the issuing bank will rebate the collector 40% of the guarantee interest, about 6% to 6.5% per annum, and the term for collecting the banknotes is two to three years. Since the Ministry of Finance announced on November 4 that the banknotes of the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications would be legal tender, the banks that issued banknotes, other than the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications, are the Zhejiang Industrial Bank, the Siming Bank, the Commercial Bank, the China Industrial Bank, the Fourth Bank, the Yih Bank, the China Agricultural Bank, the Agricultural and Commercial Bank, etc. Because the power to issue banknotes has been centralized in the Issuing Reserve Management Committee, and further issuance is restricted, the Ministry of Finance has set a deadline to gradually exchange them back with Central Bank banknotes. Therefore, the method of designated banknotes has been canceled.

Three Banks Change to Collecting Legal Tender

The Money Industry Association and various money shops collect designated banknotes, with the Central Bank as the main one. The Bank of China and the Bank of Communications have decided that the method is to use 60% cash and 40% guarantee to collect designated banknotes. Association Chairman He Zhongxiao has agreed with the Central Bank and others that the method of collecting designated banknotes will be changed to collecting legal tender. The method is still to use 60% cash and 40% guarantee to collect legal tender, and the "repurchase" method will be canceled. The term is two years, and the money industry's joint reserve will collect and distribute it to member money shops, which has already been implemented. As for the member banks of the Banking Association, those who collect designated banknotes from the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications will also handle it according to the above method of collecting legal tender.

Various Shops Oppose the Cancellation of Designated Banknotes

The Heng, Li, and Zhen money shops, which are not members of the Money Industry Association, mainly collect designated banknotes from the Fourth Bank, the Commercial Bank, and the China Industrial Bank. Their collection method is to use 100% cash to collect banknotes, and the issuing bank will rebate 40% of the guarantee interest. After the Dalu Bank and other banks canceled the designated banknote method, they immediately organized a joint office for banknote collectors, arguing on the basis of reason. In addition to filing a lawsuit against the Dalu Bank in the First Special District Court, they also requested assistance from Du Yuesheng, Tang Shoumin, Chen Guangfu, Yu Zuoting, Hu Bijiang, and others to uphold justice, believing that although the issuance has been centralized in the Issuing Reserve Management Committee, the reserves paid by the issuing banks are also 60% cash and 40% guarantee, so the banknote collection method should not be canceled. It is reported that the total amount of banknotes collected by various shops has reached more than 30 million yuan.

Agreed Method After Mediation

After Du Yuesheng, Tang Shoumin, Yu Zuoting, and others managed to mediate, the Commercial Bank, for the original contract for the collection of designated banknotes, will continue to be valid before the expiration date, but the actual amount collected by November 3 will be the standard, and the amount sealed and not collected will be reduced. The China Industrial Bank and other banks will also pay the interest on the 40% guarantee that should have been rebated last year. Now, only the Dalu Bank (note: the Dalu Bank collects Central South banknotes) and the Donglai Bank (note: the Donglai Bank collects Central Bank banknotes) have not been resolved. Tang Shoumin and Hu Bijiang are currently trying to mediate, and it is expected that it may be resolved before the end of various industries.
