Ministry of Finance Instructs Banking and Money Industries to Accept City Land Certificates as Much as Possible, with the Same Effect as Perpetual Lease Deeds, in Order to Facilitate Financial Circulation and Emphasize Land Sovereignty 96

Xinxin News Agency reports: The banking and money industries in this city have received an order from the Ministry of Finance stating that for real estate certificates, sales, and mortgages, land certificates should have the same effect as perpetual lease deeds to avoid discrimination and protect sovereignty. The banking and money industries association, after receiving the order, has already sent separate letters to various banks and firms yesterday to implement it. The original text of the instruction is recorded below: Respectfully, we recently received Instruction No. 21773 from the Ministry of Finance, stating: "Approved based on the Shanghai Municipal Government's consultation, which stated, according to the Shanghai Land Bureau's report: It has been observed that capital circulation in this city has historically relied heavily on real estate certificates for buying, selling, and mortgaging. However, since the January 28th Incident, social finance has become increasingly stagnant, the market has declined, and all industries have deteriorated, almost to the point of collapse. The underlying cause is that the banking and money industries have refused to mortgage real estate in this city, making financial turnover impossible. Real estate certificates that were once active in the market have suddenly come to a standstill. If relief is not planned, how can recovery be achieved? Recently, since the central government implemented the legal tender system, some banks have handled real estate mortgages, but they mostly only accept perpetual lease deeds, and many land lots with land certificates are still unable to obtain financing. Treating the same land lot differently based on the type of certificate is unfair. In the future, citizens holding land certificates will not only be unable to utilize them, but also lose faith in them, which will hinder the Land Bureau's future certificate renewal efforts. On the other hand, this would be equivalent to increasing the value of perpetual lease deeds, giving them an opportunity to develop. In the future, people seeking mortgage convenience will flock to convert their certificates, which will have a significant impact on our country's land sovereignty. Moreover, the Land Bureau is actively carrying out land consolidation, and the effect of land certificates and perpetual lease deeds is no different. As the Director's duty lies in protecting our country's land sovereignty and facilitating social finance, it is necessary to prevent problems before they arise and urgently report to superiors. We respectfully request that the Minister promptly issue orders to the banking and money industries in this city that handle real estate mortgages, and forward them to the Ministry of Finance, instructing them to accept land certificates as much as possible for mortgages, with the same effect as perpetual lease deeds, to avoid discrimination and protect sovereignty, as it is in the public interest." Based on this, it is understood that the Land Bureau's intention is to rescue the market from decline and find ways to facilitate finance, while also increasing the credibility of land certificates and preventing the unauthorized conversion of perpetual lease deeds, which is very commendable. This can be implemented as is. In addition to instructions, we should also consult for assistance in accepting mortgages as much as possible to maintain the market. Regarding the enforcement of auction of mortgaged real estate in this city, the Land Bureau previously proposed alternative measures, which have been separately submitted for consultation. If approved, it will be even more beneficial to those who receive mortgages. This is hereby reported and we hope to receive a response." In addition to the Ministry's order to the Shanghai Land Bureau, ordering the Shanghai banking and money industry to accept the mortgage of city land certificates with the same acceptance as perpetual lease deeds, it is to maintain the effectiveness of city land certificates and revitalize the financial situation, and should be transferred by the Shanghai Banking Association to inform all banks and companies to investigate and handle. That the Land Bureau’s presented proposals regarding Shanghai’s mortgaged real estate to implement changes in the auction method, has already been summoned by the Executive Yuan to convene various related meetings for review, and after the Yuan has reviewed and approved, an order will be sent to the ministry before being delivered. This order, and so on, is hereby issued and should be transferred to all industries to investigate and handle accordingly.

Extreme Cold in This City Yesterday 97

Lowest Temperature 18.7 Degrees; Tap Water Also Frozen

Inland River Navigation Impeded; Drastic Reduction in Incoming and Outgoing Vessels

Since the beginning of winter in this city, the weather has been mild, resembling the spring season. The cold gradually started in the afternoon the day before yesterday, and by nightfall, the weather was clear and extremely cold, with frost appearing. Yesterday morning, winter monsoon winds began to blow, and the temperature dropped sharply.

All-Day Freeze

The lowest temperature yesterday morning before sunrise was 18.7 degrees, 13 degrees below freezing. At 11:00 AM, it was 25.2 degrees. The highest temperature in the afternoon (around 1:00 PM) was 27.7 degrees. By 3:00 PM, it was 25.3 degrees. Afterward, the temperature gradually decreased, falling back to around 20 degrees, resulting in a complete lack of thawing throughout the day. Thick ice formed in streets and alleys throughout the city, creating a so-called "bottomed out" ice condition. There was slight melting around noon, but the ice quickly re-froze. Tap water pipes were also frozen.

Inland River Navigation Blocked

Due to the excessive ice, inland river vessels coming to Shanghai from inland areas were unable to operate on schedule due to the frozen rivers. For example, the Suzhou-Shanghai routes were delayed, and the Shen-Hu route also failed to arrive on time due to the ice. In addition, cargo ships on all routes were delayed, resulting in a sharp decrease in the number of rice and vegetable ships arriving in Shanghai for trade yesterday. Furthermore, the monsoon winds that started yesterday morning subsided around 4:30 PM that afternoon and are expected to return today. According to astronomical observations, the weather should moderate after two days.

Shanghai Land Bureau Announces New Method for Supplementary Land Tax and Price Payment Based on Supplementary Tax and Price Payment; Those Unable to Pay Can Repay in Installments with Added Interest 99

Since the land survey in this city, it has been found that many households have a significant amount of land exceeding the amount recorded on their title deeds. According to regulations, they must pay the price and supplement the tax before they can obtain a certificate. Since the Land Bureau drafted the standards for handling excess land in June 1934, those who exceeded or occupied land by less than three fen and were unable to pay were temporarily allowed to use the land. As a result, the number of people paying the price has gradually decreased. Recently, it was heard that the Land Bureau has formulated measures for sorting out supplementary tax and price payment and making the land complete for landowners. The previous report has been recorded, and regulations and procedures have also been drafted for handling supplementary tax matters in the future. It has been submitted to the Municipal Government for approval and announcement. The announcement and regulations are extracted below:

Announcement

Announcement by the Shanghai Land Bureau: It has been investigated that the standards for handling excess land in this city were revised in June 1934 and submitted to the Municipal Government for approval and announcement. However, it has been found that the aforementioned standards for excess land have a provision that those who exceed or occupy land by less than three fen and are unable to pay may be temporarily allowed to use the land. Therefore, all landowners have requested to follow this precedent, and only a few have complied with the order to pay the price. Since the land survey in this city, it has been found that many households have a large amount of excess land, mostly scattered and fragmented. To make the land complete for landowners, supplementary tax and price payment should be the principle. If they are truly unable to pay the price, they may pay in installments over several years to make it easier. Therefore, after considering the situation, thirteen articles of the Shanghai Land Bureau's Regulations on Supplementary Land Tax have been drafted, and detailed procedures for handling supplementary taxes for additional title deeds and beach road base lands have been formulated and submitted to the Municipal Government for approval. These regulations and procedures are hereby announced to the people of the city for their information. Except for cases that have already been handled but not concluded before October 18th, where payment notices have been issued, they should be handled in accordance with the approved methods for clearing cases of supplementary land tax that have already been handled but not concluded, and for clearing cases of beach road land that have been completed but not paid. In the future, supplementary tax cases should be handled in accordance with these regulations. Furthermore, the standards for handling excess land in this city will be abolished from the date of this announcement. Be informed accordingly. Special announcement, January of the 25th year of the Republic of China, Cai Zengji, concurrently acting director.

Regulations

Regulations on Supplementary Land Tax of the Shanghai Land Bureau: (Article 1) If the area of land measured in this city is greater than the original amount recorded on the landowner's property certificate, the excess amount shall be considered excess land. The landowner shall pay the price and supplement the tax in accordance with the provisions of these regulations. The price of the aforementioned excess land shall be calculated at 60% of the land's estimated value. The Land Bureau shall notify the landowner to pay the price after the landowner signs the drawing. (Article 2) After receiving the payment notice, the landowner shall come to the bureau to pay the price within 15 days. If they cannot pay the price within the aforementioned period, they shall state the reasons and submit them to the Land Bureau for review within this period. (Article 3) If the application in Article 2 is approved by the Land Bureau, the land price may be paid in installments over a period of time, with interest added. However, the specified period shall not exceed ten years. (Article 4) The interest payable for installment payments shall be determined in accordance with the following provisions: Residential land shall be subject to a weekly interest rate of 6%; Agricultural land shall be subject to a weekly interest rate of 4%. The term "residential land" in the preceding paragraph refers to land on which houses have been built or are being built. The term "agricultural land" refers to land used exclusively for farming or animal husbandry. The criteria for distinguishing between them shall be determined by the land conditions at the time of application for payment. (Article 5) If the ownership of land for which the price and interest payable in installments in accordance with Articles 3 and 4 have not been fully paid is to be transferred, it shall be paid in full at once, regardless of whether the installment payment period has expired. The interest in the preceding paragraph shall be calculated up to the date of payment. (Article 6) Applications submitted after receiving the payment notice to supplement field deeds or other evidence of equal validity for inclusion in the original amount calculation shall not be accepted, except when confirmed to be consistent. (Article 7) When excess and deficiency amounts are found in the land consolidation of combined title deeds, they shall not be offset against each other unless they are owned by the same person or inherited from the same ancestor and verified by the Land Bureau. (Article 8) When measuring several parcels of land with the same map number but different title deeds, the deficiency amount shall not be offset against the excess amount unless each parcel is owned by the same person. (Article 9) Those who occupied excess land before the implementation of these regulations, have already obtained a land business license but have not paid the price, regardless of whether the stamp on the license says "Price shall be paid when the house is rebuilt," or "Temporarily allowed to use, price shall be paid upon transfer," or "If rented to a foreign merchant, price shall be paid first," shall submit the land business license to the bureau within four months to pay the price or pay in installments in accordance with Articles 2, 3, and 4 of these regulations. (Article 10) The price and interest for supplementary land tax shall be listed by the Land Bureau and four copies of the receipt shall be filled out and entrusted to the Field Tax Collection Office of the Finance Bureau for collection. (Article 11) The Land Bureau may dispose of violations of Articles 2 and 9 of these regulations by effective means. The same shall apply to those who fail to comply with the procedures approved by the Land Bureau for the application in Article 2, paragraph 2 of these regulations. (Article 12) These regulations shall be implemented after being approved and announced by the Municipal Government, and the previously established standards for handling excess land shall be abolished at the same time. (Article 13) Matters not covered in these regulations may be submitted to the Municipal Government for amendment at any time.

Procedures

Procedures for handling various supplementary land tax matters by the Shanghai Land Bureau: Certificates shall be issued within one month after landowners pay the price for all types of supplementary land tax land (including supplementary title deed land and all supplementary land tax land). For cases of supplementary title deed land and public beach and road land that are not naturally generated sub-cases, public announcement procedures shall be carried out after mapmaking and before approving the supplementary tax. The method is to publish the location of the land owner, etc., in newspapers and post a topographic map at the bureau gate for the public to view. The cost of the announcement shall be borne by the applicant and may be deducted from the payment, but those who are not allowed to apply for the increase shall not be refunded. For supplementary tax cases, the land measurement fee shall be paid first, and then the measurement shall be carried out. If the supplementary tax is approved, it may be deducted at the time of payment. Those who are not allowed shall not be refunded.

Central Bank's Unlimited Buying and Selling of Foreign Exchange; Central Bank's Financial Weekly Publishes Report; Daily Newspaper Also Praises Successful Control 101

Huadong News Agency reports: Since the Ministry of Finance implemented the currency control system on November 4th last year, the unlimited buying and selling of foreign exchange has become more effective. Recently, the Central Bank's latest publication, the combined issues 2 and 3 of the Financial Weekly, details the process of maintaining foreign exchange rates by the Central Bank after the severe decline in London silver prices last year. Yesterday, the Japanese newspaper also praised the Central Bank's control effectiveness, which can curb Beiping speculation. A Huadong News Agency reporter urgently recorded the following:

Foreign Exchange Rates Remain Stable

After the London silver prices began to plummet at the end of last year, the people of Shanghai were quite uneasy, and the demand for forward foreign exchange increased sharply, and the exchange rate gradually tightened. Later, because the national bank sold foreign exchange without limit at a selling price of one shilling two pence three seven five and twenty-nine and a half yuan, showing the fullness of foreign exchange stored in England and the United States, the Shanghai foreign exchange market loosened immediately. By the first day of the week (December 30), the public's belief in the government's ability to maintain the exchange rate increased, so the foreign exchange bulls had to sell at a low price or swap to February. On Saturday (January 4), the Central Bank announced that the swap price was still three thirty-seconds of a penny and three-sixteenths of a dollar, so the number of swap transactions between various banks and the national bank was quite large. This is the effectiveness of the national bank maintaining the currency system by selling foreign exchange at a fixed buying price. Since the beginning of the new year, this trend has become more obvious. The near-term British exchange rate has risen from one shilling two pence four six eight seven five to one shilling two pence and a half, and one shilling two pence five three one two five, and the US exchange rate has actually increased step by step from twenty-nine yuan eight seven five to nine three seven five to the buying price set by the national bank. When the national bank's weekly near-term exchange rate reaches one shilling two pence six two five and the US exchange rate reaches the buying price of thirty yuan, it should be purchased without limit. According to one week, the reason why the foreign exchange trend has turned loose is that, in addition to the bulls being impatient and selling off one after another, it is also due to the prosperity of export bills of exchange, and the special amount of foreign receivables due to the Lunar New Year. However, on January 10, the US exchange rate was relatively firm, and the actual foreign exchange market reached thirty yuan, which was caused by the sharp increase in the spread between the British and US rates. According to foreign telegrams, the decline in British and US exchange rates was caused by fears in the international financial market that the United States would devalue again, but since our country's new currency system has a fixed rate for foreign exchange, any change in British and US exchange rates will not affect the national bank. It can be seen from the government's control of foreign exchange that the national bank bought as much US exchange as possible at the buying price of thirty yuan at the end of the week. At the end of last week, it was reported that the government had banned foreign exchange speculation, but in fact the government had a clear order prohibiting improper trading of foreign exchange from September 8, 1934. Now that the government controls foreign exchange by anchoring, its success is better than restriction.

Daily Newspaper Also Praises Successful Control

Yesterday's Japanese newspaper also said that the success of the three banks in controlling foreign exchange is enough to curb speculation. A special excerpt is as follows: The control is successful, and the market is unusually idle. Since the Shanghai gold market soared to 1217 yuan in early November last year, it has been rising and falling, gradually showing a downward trend. By January 15 of this year, it had fallen to 1139 yuan and 80 cents, and on January 16, even with the swap difference, it was only 1150 yuan. In two months, it actually fell by about 70 yuan. After the national government implemented the new policy, Chinese businessmen and speculators were deeply uneasy about the control, so they worked hard to buy, which caused the gold market to soar. Unexpectedly, the government's control was unexpectedly consolidated, and in addition to the settlement of swaps before the Lunar New Year, the gold market fell by 70 yuan. As for the foreign exchange market, it also relies on the government's banks to adjust at any time, and the limits of one shilling two pence six two five for the British exchange rate, thirty yuan for the US exchange rate, and one hundred and four yuan for the Japanese exchange rate can still be maintained. In recent days, the British and US foreign exchange rates have been very favorable, and the market has been selling US exchange, but the Central Bank can still maintain it, so the market has been unusually idle in recent days, and the Lunar New Year is imminent, so I think there will be no major changes in the near future.

Rescuing Tianjin Financials: 5 Million Loan About to be Disbursed, Undertaken by Seven Banks Including Bank of China, Joint Savings Society, and Bank of Communications 106

According to the Da Gong She, in order to maintain the financials of Beijing and Tianjin and overcome difficulties, the Tianjin-Beijing Financial Maintenance Committee, led by Chairman Qin Dechun and Vice Chairman Xiao Zhenying, specially borrowed 10 million from the banking sector in this city to rescue the markets of Beijing and Tianjin. All industry associations and chambers of commerce in the two places were fully responsible. This was handled by a banking consortium composed of the Bank of China, Joint Savings Society, and Bank of Communications from this city, as well as the Zhongnan Bank, Continental Bank, Jin Cheng Bank, and Salt Industry Bank. 5 million for the Beijing market has already been disbursed by the seven banks, and the 5 million for the Tianjin market has also been successfully negotiated. The seven banks including Bank of China, Joint Savings Society, and Bank of Communications, Zhongnan Bank, Continental Bank, Jin Cheng Bank, and Salt Industry Bank, will instruct their Tianjin branches to allocate the funds. The distribution of the funds is as follows: the Central Bank will bear 1.5 million, and the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications will each bear 1 million, totaling 3.5 million. The remaining four banks will jointly contribute 1.5 million, bringing the total to 5 million, which will be handed over to the Tianjin-Beijing Financial Maintenance Committee to be re-lent to various merchants and money shops in Tianjin. It is said that these loans are all of a temporary nature.

Sino-Belgian Gengkuan Committee: Continuing University Thesis Awards, Initial Award Money Proved Quite Effective, This Year's Topics Focus on Science 107

The Sino-Belgian Gengkuan Committee decided in a general meeting the year before last to allocate 3,000 yuan to administer university thesis awards. At the time, students in graduating classes from universities across the country submitted their work enthusiastically, resulting in a wealth of excellent pieces. The committee organized a judging panel which selected many winners, distributing a total of 1,700 yuan in awards. The remaining 1,300 yuan will be used to continue the essay competition this year. The committee's secretariat has already sent letters to various universities across the country. The official letter and essay topics are excerpted below:

Notice to All Schools: To encourage academic research, our committee decided in a previous general meeting to allocate 3,000 silver dollars as a university thesis fund for China. The selection of thesis topics and judging matters are handled by a sub-committee of experts appointed by our committee. The results of implementation in the 22nd year of the Republic were quite successful. This year, we will continue to use the remaining funds to administer the program. We have appointed experts who have proposed topics. In addition to publishing them in the newspapers, we are enclosing a copy of the thesis award regulations and detailed rules, as well as a copy of the thesis topics for each science department, for your school's reference. We hope you will announce this widely to all and maintain our public friendship. Sincerely, Chairman Chu Minyi

Thesis Topics: University Thesis Award Topics for the Second Session of the Sino-Belgian Gengkuan Committee. (A) Topics for the Department of Engineering Materials and Mechanical Engineering: Methods of mechanical power transmission on vehicles and in factories. Mechanical transmission of power on vehicles and in factories. What kind of primary power source is suitable for a factory with defense characteristics, and how should it be designed? Please discuss. (B) Topics for the Department of Agricultural Science (Cotton): The current state of the cotton industry in China and methods for its improvement. Cotton industry and national defense. (C) Topics for the Department of Physical Sciences: A catalogue and summary of physics papers published by Chinese physicists at home and abroad. A detailed description of various studies on the construction of the atomic nucleus. Raman Effect and molecular construction. (D) Topics for the Department of Law: The distinction and relationship between law and morality. Discuss the principles of law based on the establishment and revocation of contracts. What are the reasons that English and American scholars do not recognize the binding force of treaties, while the continent does? (E) Topics for the Department of Business (Accounting): An outline of cost accounting for spinning and weaving mills. Account books are tools for recording the increase and decrease of business owners' property, so the subject of bookkeeping should be subjective. Since the introduction of European and American value recording into China, the accounting subject has become the subject of journal entries, and thus has become objective bookkeeping, while the lending relationship of the business owner is often hidden and not expressed. However, the cash journal method of daily accounting, and the British-style asset and liability statement, are partly subjective recording methods. The common objective accounting method has failed to be consistent from beginning to end, while our country's inherent account books, although their form still has many shortcomings, have always used the receipt and payment of money as the subject of bookkeeping. All receipts are entered into receipts, and all payments are entered into payments, which is consistent from daily settlement to settlement report, is easy to understand, and conforms to the nature of account books. This is a unique feature of our country's accounting. Please study its theoretical and factual basis using scientific methods, and make a detailed comparison of subjective and objective bookkeeping methods. (F) Topics for the Department of Medical Science (Hygiene): The relationship between public health and people's livelihood. How should my country's entire medical and health construction be planned and implemented?

Implementing Regulations on Prohibition of Opium and Drugs, the Shanghai Municipal Council Actually Expresses Opposition, Prosecution of Opium and Drug Cases Still Prosecuted Under the Old Criminal Law, Deliberate Steps Taken to Deal with the Court Are Incomprehensible 113

In order to implement the government's laws and regulations and ban opium and drugs within the time limit, the Shanghai First Special District Local Court has, since the 14th of this month, applied the two regulations on prohibition of opium and drugs promulgated by the Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission and concurrently the Director General of Opium Prohibition to all opium and drug cases brought by the Shanghai Municipal Council under the opium crime provisions of the Criminal Code. Originally, those who operated opium and drugs and those who had opium and drug addictions in the Public Concession saw that the previous opium bans had been incomplete and that the government's laws and regulations were not implemented in the Concession, so they thought that this time would follow the same path and they were all at ease. Although some people applied to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for registration and licenses, less than one in a hundred did so. Now, the First Special Court has been able to overcome all kinds of difficulties and resolutely punish opium and drug offenders in accordance with the regulations, which is truly effective for the future of opium prohibition, and the opium addicts in the Concession must also have a sense of being punished. In the future, there will be no shortage of people who will automatically repent. Unexpectedly, at the beginning of this implementation, the Shanghai Municipal Council, which has the heavy responsibility of reporting, suddenly raised objections. The Council determined that the two regulations on opium and drug prohibition are not formal laws of our country, so the opium and drug cases handed over to the court by the police stations are still prosecuted in accordance with the opium provisions of the Criminal Code, but the judge said that the chapter on opium crimes has been expressly abolished by the government and is not applicable. Therefore, the punishment is meted out in accordance with the provisions of the regulations on opium and drug prohibition. However, the Council has now expressed its opposition and has drafted several countermeasures. It is said that its first step is that anyone convicted under the regulations on opium and drug prohibition will be directly sent by the court to the Caohejing Prison for execution, and the Council will not be responsible for enforcement. The second and third steps it has drafted are even more resolute. However, the central government's current opium prohibition policy has long been deeply praised internationally, which shows that the harm of opium and drugs is deeply hated by all sectors of the world. The authorities of the Concession have always been known for their wisdom, and their hatred of opium and drugs is no less than that of our government and people. Now, it is unknown whether there is a slight misunderstanding in prosecuting opium and drug cases without complying with the newly issued regulations. Otherwise, it would not hate what good people hate. It is expected that the misunderstanding will be eliminated soon and they will still be able to cooperate with the court. Therefore, no matter how difficult it feels, the court will never be discouraged.

Mr. Ding Wenjiang, a well-known geologist and director-general of the National Academia Sinica in our country, has passed away in Hunan. The colleagues of the Academy are deeply shocked and saddened. Memorial Service in Beijing and Shanghai Today

The memorial service prepared by the Academy is scheduled to be held simultaneously in Beijing and Shanghai at 2:00 PM today. Establish Academic Research Scholarship

Last Night: Fire on Kangti Road, More Than 20 Civilian Houses Destroyed, Has Not Been Extinguished as of 1:00 AM This Morning 117

At around 10:00 PM last night, a major fire broke out on Kangti Road in the French Concession, destroying more than 20 civilian houses and factory buildings. The French Concession Fire Department was fully dispatched to put out the fire, which has not been completely extinguished as of 1:00 AM this morning. The details are recorded below:

Wind Boosts the Fire The Feijia Lane area behind Sideri on Kangti Road in the French Concession (east of the Sapo Hotel) is densely populated, mostly by coolies and workers, mostly civilians. There is a Republican Printing and Dyeing Factory, so half of the nearby residents work in the factory. At around 10:10 PM last night, a charcoal ball shop suddenly reported carelessness. At that time, the north wind was blowing, and the fire spread rapidly and was out of control. The first to bear the brunt was the Republican Factory. In addition, it was late at night, and the residents were all asleep. Because the area was secluded, the shops had already closed. When the fire spread, the first to discover it was only the owner of a fried rice shop.

Unapproachable

After discovering the fire, the owner of the fried rice shop immediately ran to the post office at the intersection of Sapo Hotel Road and borrowed a phone to call the fire department. At the same time, he frantically blew the police whistle. As a result, one whistle led to a hundred whistles, and the residents were awakened from their dreams. Seeing that the fire was out of control, they supported the old and carried the young, carrying boxes and bags, and fled in all directions.

Extinguished This Morning Within ten minutes, the fire departments from all roads arrived one after another. They first tried to melt the frozen hydrants by the roadside. There were a total of two pumper trucks, which fired at the same time. However, although the water pressure was strong, the fire was too big, making it difficult to put out. The fire has been shooting until about 1:00 AM this morning and has not been completely extinguished.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Introduces Yiwu Local Sugar 118

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the industry association yesterday, saying: Dear Sir, on the 16th of this month, we received a letter from the Chamber of Commerce of Fodang Town, Yiwu County, Zhejiang Province, which stated that our county's local brown sugar has a long history and has gradually expanded in recent years, with an increase in production volume. It is estimated that the total production of the county is worth about 700,000 to 800,000 yuan per year, which is of great importance to the rural economy. However, because the traditional manufacturing methods are simple and crude, the products cannot be very refined and the sales are not widespread. This year, with the approval of the county government, our association strictly rectified the production, on the one hand, prohibiting the mixing of fake products, and on the other hand, guiding the improvement of manufacturing methods. As a result, the products are pure, high-quality, and have a good taste and color. The top-quality products are better than those from Taiwan. However, its price is much lower than that of Taiwan. This year, some sugar merchants in Shanghai and Nanjing have also purchased from Yiwu and said that they are suitable for use. If the sales can be promoted, it will not only greatly benefit the rural economy of our county, but also prevent the outflow of rights and interests and block a loophole for the country. The sugar industry is now on the market, and the production volume is particularly abundant compared to previous years. We are deeply afraid that the sales will be narrow and the production will be excessive, which will cause the people to suffer. It is a great responsibility to the government's intention to promote local products and revitalize the countryside. In addition to sending samples to the higher-level authorities to order all chambers of commerce to inform their members to assist in sales, we have enclosed a sample of goods and sent it to your association, approving the sending of the Shanghai Municipal National Products Department Store and informing your members to assist in sales to benefit the industry and save the countryside. We are very grateful, etc. With this approval, we will send a box of sample sugar to the product showroom of our association. We will also send a letter to you, hoping that your association will check and notify your colleagues to promote sales vigorously to help the industry and save the countryside, etc.

Yesterday morning at approximately 5:30 AM, Rong hired a private carriage and was passing near the Ya Feng Bookstore on Route Gustale Guilemet in the French Concession when two robbers suddenly jumped out from the roadside, brandishing pistols and threatening him to remain silent. Just as they were about to begin searching and robbing him, Rong leaped from the carriage, shouting for help to catch the thieves. Seeing the situation was unfavorable, the robbers scattered and fled in different directions, firing three shots into the air as a warning. By the time nearby police officers arrived after hearing the gunshots, the robbers were long gone without a trace. Although the victim, Rong Yongming, did not suffer any losses, he was greatly frightened.

The Shanghai First Special District Citizens' Federation sent a letter yesterday to the Public Works Department of the Public Concession, requesting the allocation of funds to aid impoverished rickshaw pullers. Railway Bureau Orders All Stations to Inspect Air Brake Hoses to Avoid Delaying Train Schedules 125

Each train car conductor should have one throat-nipple type air brake hose (female thread) and one throat-straight type air brake hose (male thread) available inside the car for replacement in case the hoses are damaged during the train journey. This has long been stipulated in the traffic regulations. However, recently, the Jin-Hu and Hu-Hang Railway Bureaus have found that the hoses kept inside the car conductors' cars are either damaged, incomplete in style, or not even prepared, so there is no way to use them when the rubber hose is damaged, delaying the train running time and hindering the safety of the train. For safety reasons, the Railway Bureau has decided that from January 13 to 19, station managers at Nanjing, Nanjing Jiangbian, Zhenjiang, Changzhou, Wuxi, Suzhou, Maigen Road Freight Station, North Shanghai, South Shanghai, Jiaxing, Hangzhou, Zhakou, and Gongchenqiao stations will inspect the rubber hoses stored at the stations one by one. Those that are damaged should be exchanged immediately for the straight-head and bent-head types. If the numbers cannot be averaged, then a list of the number to be replenished should be made out and claimed from the office. The ones in good condition will be tied up with rope, with one bent head and one straight head as a pair, and properly lead-sealed to prove they are in good condition. From then on, the following measures will be implemented: Each car conductor's car should have one pair of air brake rubber hoses. If the car conductor's car has no car conductor on duty, it will be kept by the rear car conductor. When the car conductor is on duty, he should first check whether the air brake rubber hose prepared in the car conductor's car is complete and in good condition. If it is found that the lead seal is lost, or the binding is loose, or there is suspicion of damage, he should immediately declare the replacement to the on-duty station manager. When the train arrives at the terminal station, when the station manager counts the air brake rubber hose, if it is found that there is evidence of use, the conductor on duty should be asked to explain the details, and the rubber hose should be re-inspected. The ones in good condition will still be tied and sealed according to the formula, and the damaged ones will be replaced. If there is a need to replace the air hose during the train journey, the conductor on duty should report the situation to the station manager at the terminal station and record it in the conductor's report. The damaged pipe that is replaced should be replaced with a new pipe by the conductor at the nearest stop that has the pipe. The air brake rubber hose should be kept away from moisture or fire.

Yu Jiesan Invents Fire Extinguishing Powder; Experimented Yesterday at the Public Sports Field; The Powder Extinguishes Fire Quickly and Effectively; Plans to Establish a Branch Factory in Shanghai to Produce the Powder 131

According to the Guowen News Agency, Yu Jiesan, a native of Northeast China, invented fire extinguishing powder. Yesterday, he cordially invited representatives from all walks of life to conduct a fire extinguishing experiment at the Public Sports Field in Nanshi. Li Dachao, a representative from the Municipal Government; Wu Huanru, from the Social Affairs Bureau; Dong Zhihe, from the Fire Brigade of the Municipal Public Security Bureau; Wang Ziyao, a former staff officer of the Northeast Army; Shi Bingyan, the general manager of the fire extinguishing powder in South China; representatives from the South District Fire Brigade; and more than 2,000 spectators attended. The experiment started at 3:30 PM and lasted for half an hour. The process is recorded as follows:

Experiment Process

In advance, a wooden frame measuring twelve feet square was erected in the Public Sports Field in Nanshi, with wooden strips nailed on it and covered with waste paper. At 3:30 PM, representatives from all walks of life arrived. First, a photo was taken, and then a technician poured kerosene on the wooden frame and ignited it with fire. In an instant, the raging flames soared into the air. Because the wind was very strong yesterday, even though it was only a square foot of land, the smoke reached the sky, and it looked like a single building was on fire. Then, two people held fire extinguishing powder and vigorously sprinkled it on the blazing fire. The fire was extinguished and the smoke dissipated where the powder landed. In a few seconds, it was completely extinguished. The representatives then dispersed amidst the applause of the audience. It is indeed a very agile fire extinguishing tool.

Inventor's Remarks

According to inventor Yu Jiesan, the reporter said that he was formerly from the military. After resigning, he lived overseas. When traveling in Japan, he felt that the fire extinguishers in that country were very effective and was very interested in seeing the fire extinguishing powder. He bought several cans and brought them back to China. He studied them carefully, expending all his energy, but could not find the secret. So, he bought British and Italian fire extinguishing powders for comparison, analysis, and experimentation before discovering their chemical effects. He studied them even more and finally succeeded. He was originally from Northeast China and had a meager fortune. Due to his research on this fire extinguishing powder, his family property was exhausted, costing him a total of 60,000 to 70,000 yuan. Later, when the powder was completed, with the help of friends, he set up a factory to produce and sell it, naming it Zhengda Fire Extinguishing Powder. On the one hand, he registered the patent with the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, and on the other hand, he set up a factory to promote the products. At present, in South China, he is trying to promote it. There are currently three manufacturing plants in North China, one in Pingji and one in Zhangjiakou. The total number of employees is about 600. It is planned to set up a branch factory in Shanghai in the future to strive to stop the most unfortunate fire in the world. As for the properties of the powder, it is harmless to the human body, even if it enters the mouth. Because the largest component of its powder is made of baking soda, etc.

Chen Dimin and Wife Reconcile and Separate Settlement Established 133

Chen Dimin, a wealthy businessman from Anhui residing at No. 379 Beile Road in the French Concession and the owner of Lafaytte Apartments who once worked as a compradore for a foreign company, is currently 44 years old. He married Tan Kunfan, a woman from Suzhou, in his early years. They have been married for 20 years and have five children: two sons and three daughters. Because Chen took a concubine outside, opinions occurred between the husband and wife. On February 27 of last year, they argued and Chen assaulted his wife, injuring her corner of the eye. His wife, Chen Tan Kunfan, believed that her husband had become abnormal and tyrannical and could no longer live with him. She took the children and returned to her mother's home. She also reported Chen's injury to the French police. The police department filed a public prosecution against Chen with the Second Special Court. After two trials, Chen was fined. Chen Tan Kunfan then hired lawyer Jiang Yiping to file a separate settlement lawsuit against Chen Dimin in the civil division of the Second Special Court and requested the return of 700 yuan per month for nine months of living expenses away from home, totaling 6,300 yuan, and a loan of 3,000 taels. The court approved the motion. After Judge Li Liang held several court hearings and summoned witnesses, the defendant Chen Dimin appointed lawyer E Sen to defend him. The court advised the two parties to negotiate a settlement outside of court and rescheduled the hearing, as reported in this newspaper. Yesterday, both parties and their lawyers were summoned to court again. Chen's elderly mother and relatives of both parties, both male and female, also attended the hearing. First, the plaintiff's lawyer submitted a paper outlining the terms of the settlement, totaling seven items. After the court reviewed them, the opinions of the plaintiff and defendant were found to be different and not yet close. After the court painstakingly advised both parties for two hours, explaining each term of the settlement, both parties finally agreed to the terms of the settlement. The main points were: (1) The defendant agreed to the plaintiff taking the children and separating for four months. After the period, the plaintiff would take the children home to live together or form a separate small family. (2) During the separation period, the defendant would pay the plaintiff living expenses (including rent and other expenses for the children) totaling 370 yuan per month. (3) The children's education expenses would be borne by the defendant. (4) The defendant admitted to the plaintiff's expenses for the ten months away from home (i.e., the 6,300 yuan sued for) as 4,000 yuan, and would repay it with money whenever it was available. (5) The plaintiff abandoned the 3,000 taels loan lawsuit, and the defendant agreed to give the plaintiff 4,000 yuan if there was a profit of over 10,000 yuan from the sale of property in the future. (6) The defendant would give half of the Lafaytte Apartments property to the children, managed by the defendant and supervised by the plaintiff. (7) During the separation period, the plaintiff could take household items for use. Finally, the plaintiff stated that she had borrowed money for use since leaving home and needed money to pay for the New Year and pay the interest on the loan, requesting the court to order the defendant to pay 500 yuan in advance. The defendant said that his financial situation this year was very difficult and he could only pay 100 yuan first. The two parties insisted that the amount could not be resolved. The defendant then increased the amount to 200 yuan. The plaintiff said that this amount was not enough to spend and use. After the court advised him, the defendant was ordered to pay 200 yuan before the lunar New Year and another 200 yuan on the second day of the lunar New Year. The plaintiff then agreed. The clerk then made a written record of the settlement, which was signed by both parties and their lawyers, and they left the court. A husband and wife lawsuit came to an end.

Progress of the Sino-Western Pharmacy Is General 134

In this year of economic downturn, all industries are in decline, bankruptcies are common, and it is even more difficult for new pharmacies to maintain themselves in the face of competition from imported products. The pharmacy's retail department has been crowded with customers for several days, which is more lively than the four major companies. The staff treats customers with great humility, which shows that the development of the pharmacy is not accidental.

Both Railway Bureaus Approve Track Inspectors and Police to Use White Signal Lights at Night; Both Army Armored Vehicle Battalions Have Been Notified 136

Track inspectors and police on the Jin-Hu and Hu-Hangyong Railways previously used green lights at night to indicate safety signals at the request of the armored vehicle teams to make it easier to identify people moving along the tracks. The Traffic Safety Committee of both railways believes that from the perspective of railway operation, there is no need to display safety signals everywhere along the line unless there are obstacles. Conversely, in the event of an accident, track inspectors and police can follow the regulations to display temporary danger signals so that trains can stop safely. Now, the green lights displayed by track inspectors and police along the line at night have nothing to do with traffic safety. Within the station boundaries, they are confused with the signals of the trackmen, making them difficult to identify. Therefore, it is planned to order track inspectors and police along the entire line to use white lights at night to show the difference, indicate safety, and provide a warning. This has been approved by the two railway bureaus and the Second Company of the Army Armored East Detachment has been requested to notify the district teams stationed along the two railways.

###祥生 Taxi Company to Face Strict Crackdown

Since the municipal government and various bureaus and departments moved to the city center, citizens traveling to that area have had to hire taxis. Regarding the issue of fares, the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau had already convened a meeting with representatives from various bureaus and departments to decide that for taxi companies establishing branches in the city center, taxis traveling from anywhere within the city (except Caohejing) to the city center would charge a flat rate of one yuan per one-way trip. At that time, Mr. Zhou Xiangsheng, manager of the Xiangsheng Automobile Company, was also invited to attend as a representative of the trade association. He expressed his willingness to comply with the decision on the spot. Subsequently, the company applied to establish a branch on Guohua Road, and the bureau approved it. However, after receiving the license, the company then published an announcement stating that the fare was one yuan, limited to twenty minutes, and that charges beyond that limit would be handled according to industry regulations. The bureau considered this announcement to be a reversal of the previous agreement and immediately ordered a correction. The company also responded with a submission stating that it would comply. However, the Public Utilities Bureau continued to receive reports from various sources that the company was not following the regulations. In reality, it still charged one yuan and five jiao for a single trip, and there were also instances where the company refused to dispatch cars when requested by phone. After investigation, these facts were confirmed. Considering the company's disregard for regulations, a plan to crack down on it was being considered. Suddenly, the company published another announcement canceling the Guohua Road branch and stating that the minimum fare for hiring a car to the city center would be one yuan and five jiao. In order to conduct a fair and thorough investigation, the bureau sent personnel to join with staff from the Public Works Bureau to hire Xiangsheng taxis for three trips: first, from the intersection of Yangshupu Ningguo Road to Zhaofeng Park; second, from Xujiahui to Ningguo Road; and finally, from Ningguo Road back to the city center. The first two trips took 29 and 27 minutes respectively, with each trip exceeding twenty minutes and covering eight to nine miles. The company charged only one yuan for each. However, the last trip, from Ningguo Road to the city center, took only fifteen minutes, covering only four miles, but the company charged one yuan and five jiao. After receiving these reports, the bureau convened a meeting with various bureaus and departments of the municipal government. The company's claims of high gasoline prices and violations of industry regulations were deemed to be mere excuses and attempts at deception. This behavior was considered to be a major hindrance to the construction of the city center. All bureaus and departments agreed that the company had made a prior commitment but repeatedly reneged on it, abandoning its promises and disregarding regulations, and that strict measures should be taken. It is reported that a plan for a crackdown has been agreed upon and will be implemented soon.

Electrical Manufacturing Association Announces Cancellation of Patent for Silver Light Bulbs 137

According to Xin Sheng She, the Shanghai Electrical Manufacturing Industry Association has issued a notice to electrical manufacturers nationwide regarding the cancellation of the patent for silver light bulbs. The notice states that the association has received letters from member factories inquiring about whether they can imitate the silver light bulbs. After investigation, the silver light bulb is simply a renaming of the silver-plated light bulb that has been available in Belgium for two years. Previously, Mr. Wang Meiqing and others had raised objections with the ministry regarding this, and on December 5th of last year, the ministry approved the objection, canceling the patent granted to Li Qingxiang for the so-called invention of the silver light bulb. Therefore, all factories are now free to manufacture silver light bulbs. This notice is specifically issued to inform all colleagues nationwide of the truth.

Sports News

Western Football Association Revises Important Rules 143

No more than ten teams per league from next season. Revisions to the rules for the Junior Tiffin Cup tournaments. The Senior Cup competition is expected to resume next season.

The Shanghai Western Football Association recently issued a notice from Secretary Sipeke to member teams stating that the association's various rules were carefully discussed at a committee meeting held on the 20th of last month. Revisions were made to the issues of promotion and relegation of members in each league, as well as the association's articles of association, league rules, and cup competition rules. The new rules will be implemented starting next season.

Restrictions on the number of teams and promotion/relegation: At the end of each season, the two teams with the worst performance in each league, except for the First Division (who can still join their current league in the next season), must be relegated, while the two best teams can be promoted to the higher league. At the same time, starting from next season, the number of competing teams in each league shall not exceed ten, and there shall not be two teams with the same name in each league.

Start of the season and organization of the executive committee: The start of each football season was originally set from October 1st to March 31st of the following year, as stated in Article 16 of the association's articles of association. This article has now been revised by the committee to start from the last Saturday of September each year and end on the second Saturday of April of the following year. The organizational law of the Executive Committee in Article 14 has been revised to form an Executive Committee consisting of four members selected by the officials of the Western Football Association, three members of the association, one member of the British Army or British Navy, and one member of the Referee Association. Five committee members will constitute a quorum. The addition of one member from the Referee Association is new and was not present in the original articles of association.

Second Division can select four "floating players": Article 6 of the league rules has now been amended to read, "Any team participating in the league with both First and Second Divisions must select four 'Floating Players' from the Second Division and register them with the secretary of the Western Association. These four floating players can participate in matches in any league without further approval from the committee." The original article stated that any player who has participated in more than three matches in the First Division during the season cannot participate in the Second Division again, unless specially permitted by the committee. This restriction has now been removed by the amendment. However, as these four "floating players" are selected from the Second Division, there are still restrictions on the participation of First Division players in the Second Division.

Restrictions on the level of participation in cup competitions: The Western Association Senior Cup has been held only four times since it began in 1927, and was suspended in 1931. It has now been four years since it was held, and the Western Association plans to revive it next season. This committee has made revisions to the rules for the Senior, Junior, and Tiffin Cups. Article 2 of the Senior Cup rules originally stated that "all members of the Western Football Association who have not joined the league can join". It has now been revised to read "The Senior Cup competition is only open to teams in the First Division, with the winner determined by an elimination system." Article 2 of the Junior Cup rules originally stated "Only teams from the Third and Fifth Divisions and members of the Western Football Association who have not joined the league can participate." The original text of Article 1 of the Tiffin Cup rules, "All teams except those in the First Division can participate," has also been revised to read, "Only teams from the Second and Third Divisions can participate." At the same time, in Article 2 of the rules, the restriction "Players participating in the Tiffin Cup competition are not allowed to participate in the Junior Cup competition" has been added. The original text of this article was "Players who have participated in more than three matches in the First Division cannot participate at will."

For Western League football, today's First Division match is Recreation vs. Jewish, starting at 3:00 PM at Shen Yuan. Children's Educational Novel

Little Men (I) (V) (V) 164

— Original by Louisa M. Alcott, Translated by Zheng Xiaocang

Poor Nat, having suffered this setback, suffered a spiritual wound that would never heal. He felt that he had not only lost his partnership and protector, but also that his personality had gone bankrupt, and that he had lost his identity in the trading arena from then on. No one could trust his words anymore, whether spoken or written, even if he tried his best to redeem his past hypocrisy; the sign had been taken down, the company had been dismantled, and he was a fallen and ruined man. That warehouse, – the Wall Street of the children (note) – no longer knew Nat’s name. Wrinkled Forehead and her several sisters cried earnestly, as if wanting his favor, yet he finally did not come, and seemed to truly sympathize with his misfortune, because the eggs laid were decreasing day by day, and several chickens were annoyed, and retreated to new nests that Tom could not find.

Nat heard this news and said, "They believe me;" although several children who heard it sneered, Nat used it to comfort himself, because when a person is down on his luck, even the trust of a speckled old hen feels extremely comforting.

However, Tom did not look for a new partner, because suspicion had seeped in, and the previous intimacy of confiding in each other no longer existed. Ned expressed his willingness to partner, but he also declined, and the fair attitude in his words showed that he was indeed a man of integrity. He said:

"Maybe it will be discovered that Nat didn't take the money, then we can partner again. I think this is unlikely, but we have to give him a chance and leave this position open for a little longer."

(Note) Wall Street is the area where New York bankers gather daily, holding the reins of American commerce; it is used here metaphorically.

Commercial News

Finance: Silver Bull Market Breaks Through 20 Pence Barrier; Standard Silver Makes Steady Progress; Briefly Breaks 70 Yuan Barrier; Ultimately Soars 17 Yuan; Bulls Exceed 34 165

Yesterday, the gold market saw a surge in buying interest as spot silver broke through the 20 pence barrier, disappointing the shorts. Coupled with the Commercial Bank of China’s frantic purchases of US dollars, prices soared to over 70 yuan before becoming erratic. In the morning, the overseas silver market saw contractions in both the UK and US, leading to the expectation that spot silver would fall. It was said that after the market closed, the US Treasury Department purchased a portion of silver in its sales quantity at the listed price, but there were still sellers at around 0.1875 below the listed price, with no buyers. Forward silver prices in Monterrey fell between 0.09 and 0.015. Exchange rates contracted slightly. London spot gold rose by half a penny. The public's sentiment was bullish, as silver had broken the 20 pence barrier, and pessimism about crossing the barrier further fueled buying interest. When the over-the-counter grey market opened, it immediately rose to 52.53 yuan, with Chun Yuan, Yong Shun, and Mao Lai entering. At this time, the market was balanced with buyers selling and supply was lacking. Chun Yuan, Yong Shun, Mao Fu Xing, Yong Ri, Chang Da De Cheng, Hui Xiang, Heng Jing, Yong Ding, Kang Li, and Feng Ju advanced, rising gradually. Buying interest was at its peak. The People's Bank of China’s listed rates were announced, with both the UK and US unchanged, and the customs gold unit remained unchanged. The standard silver price was listed at 1145.2 yuan, with little impact. The morning opening was the highest, and although there was some downstream selling after the opening, the buyers were eager to buy at lower prices, allowing the price to rise. The Hong Kong and Shanghai Banking Corporation’s listed rates were announced, with both the UK and US unchanged. There was considerable fluctuation at this point. Later, the Commercial Bank of China and others frantically purchased US dollars, boosting public sentiment and breaking through the 60 yuan barrier, continuing to report gains. The silver balancing tax was announced to have fallen by 0.0125 (only 4% being levied). Although there was a small setback after the high, the exchange market was still difficult to ease, buying interest was easily ignited, the trading floor was dry, and the situation remained strong. Major players rushed to buy, briefly approaching the 70 yuan barrier. Banks took advantage of the high prices to sell slightly, and suppliers were active at the high prices. There was a temporary dip, but public sentiment remained strong. The upward trend continued at midday. In the after-hours market, although there was a slight setback from over 70 yuan, buying interest remained strong, and the price finally rose to a high of 72.4 yuan. Banks sold in droves. Reuters reported that the US House of Representatives was scheduled to meet on the 17th to discuss raising silver prices, which immediately triggered a sell-off, falling back almost 10 yuan. Indian silver initially reported a contraction of 5 annas, and then recovered slightly after the low. The overall trend has stabilized, but public sentiment is extremely erratic, as is the market movement. Here is a record of today's market conditions:

The morning opening was 1157 yuan, up 8.2 yuan from the previous close. Yuan Chang, Yong Da, De Cheng, and Heng Yu sold off, retreating from 7.2 yuan to 5.3 yuan. Ding Tai, Da Fa, and Yong Li bought, rising to 7.7 yuan. Chun Yuan and Yong Heng Yu sold off, falling to 7 yuan. Ding Kang and Hui Xiang advanced again to 7.8 yuan. Qing Fa, Yong Qian, Yuan Yong, Tong Tai Chang, Fu Xing Yong, Hong Kang Yong, Yuan Mao Yong took advantage of the high prices to sell, falling to 6.1 yuan. Chun Yuan, Yong Fu Xing Yong, and Ding Kang entered, rising to 8 yuan. Although Da De Cheng and De Li sold, Fu Xing Yong, Ju Da, Hui Xiang, and Ding Kang continued to advance, rising to 9.8 yuan. Fu Xing Yong, Zhen Tai, and Yuan Mao Yong sold to 8.8 yuan. Ri Chang, Tong Fu, Ju Da, and Qing Fa Yong advanced again to 9.6 yuan. Hui Xiang, Tong Tai Chang, Da De Cheng, and Qia Feng Yong Shun sold off, falling to 7.2 yuan. Heng Yu, Ding Kang, and Da De Cheng floated and bought in a rush. China National Aviation Corporation continued to buy spot US dollars at 875, breaking through the 60 yuan barrier and rising to 61.4 yuan. Oil Market - The Oil Market of the Past Year - Can Be Divided into Three Segments - Soybean Oil Differs by More Than Ten Yuan - Crude Oil Also Has More Than Six Yuan and Four Jiao 175

The market price trend of soybean oil and peanut oil in the twenty-fourth year can be divided into three segments. From February 8th (i.e., the fifth day of the lunar New Year) to the end of April, it was generally stable. Because arrivals and sales were balanced, there were no unexpected disturbances. From May to September, it was entirely in a sluggish state. At this time, arrivals surged and sales were weak. Affected by the economic downturn in various parties, the first ten days of September were the most depressed. From October to December, due to the fatigue from above, buyers took advantage of the cheapness and moved again. Investigation - The Origin of the Decline of the Tianjin Weaving Industry 178

(Tianjin Correspondence) The weaving industry and the carpet industry in this city are both important local handicrafts. During the years of the Republic of China 18 and 19, there were more than 400 weaving factories, large and small, with more than 10,000 workers. After the Republic of China 20, it gradually declined. By the number of factories in the previous year, although still maintaining more than 300, the number of workers has decreased by more than seventy percent. By last year, it was getting worse. During the summer and autumn, the number of machines stopped accounted for as much as 80 percent. Also, each factory dismissed workers and apprentices to save expenses. By the autumn and winter seasons, business slightly turned. According to people in the industry, the biggest reason for the decline of native cloth is the oppression from foreign cloth. According to the general sales price of foreign cloth, compared with the cost of local cotton yarn, it is already about the same. Therefore, after weaving, the quality is below foreign goods, and the selling price is above foreign goods. Relatively speaking, it is impossible to exist.
